### [Sessão Paralela: PM]
Vou definir os KPIs e priorizar as features premium. Primeiro, preciso entender:

Qual é o principal problema de estabilidade atual que os usuários relatam?

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Arquitetura de Refatoração

## 1. ADR-001: Estratégia de Arquitetura V10

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Backend

### CONTEXTO:
A V9 do DIYAPP evoluiu organicamente para uma arquitetura monolítica com acoplamento alto entre módulos. A manutenção tornou-se complexa, deploys são arriscados e a escalabilidade é limitada. Precisamos definir uma arquitetura sustentável para V10 que permita:
- Desenvolvimento paralelo de squads
- Deploys independentes
- Escalabilidade seletiva por componente
- Manutenção simplificada

### DECISÃO:
Adotaremos uma arquitetura **Microsserviços Estratégicos com Núcleo Monolítico** (Modular Monolith First, com caminho para microsserviços).

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A: Microsserviços Puros** - Cada domínio como serviço independente
  - Prós: Escalabilidade máxima, deploys independentes, tecnologia heterogênea
  - Contras: Complexidade operacional alta, latência de rede, consistência distribuída difícil
  - Custo: 8-12 meses para migração completa

- **Opção B: Monolito Modular (escolhida)** - Estrutura interna de módulos com boundaries claros
  - Prós: Manutenção simplificada, deploys únicos, consistência transacional
  - Contras: Escalabilidade limitada ao servidor único inicialmente
  - Custo: 3-4 meses para refatoração

- **Opção C: Arquitetura Híbrida** - Núcleo monolítico + serviços específicos
  - Prós: Balanceamento entre complexidade e benefícios
  - Contras: Gerenciamento de duas arquiteturas
  - Custo: 5-6 meses

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Refatoração incremental sem downtime
- Módulos podem evoluir para microsserviços quando necessário
- Time to market mais rápido para V10
- Redução de 60% no acoplamento inicial

**Negativas:**
- Escalabilidade vertical inicial (horizontal após migração para serviços)
- Deploy único inicial (canary releases via feature flags)

**Riscos:**
- Módulos podem manter acoplamento se boundaries não forem respeitados
- Mitigação: Contract Tests entre módulos + validação em CI/CD

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15 (3 meses após implementação)

---

## 2. Engineering Standards V10

```yaml
# .github/engineering-standards.yml
version: '1.0'
last_updated: 2024-01-15

# 1. ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO
project_structure:
  pattern: "feature-based"
  layers:
    - presentation: "UI/controllers"
    - application: "Use cases/services"
    - domain: "Business entities"
    - infrastructure: "DB/external services"
  
  directories:
    - src/
      - modules/          # Módulos independentes
        - auth/           # Exemplo: módulo de autenticação
          - application/
          - domain/
          - infrastructure/
          - presentation/
          - tests/
      - shared/           # Código compartilhado entre módulos
        - kernel/         # Core do framework
        - common/         # Utilitários
        - contracts/      # Interfaces entre módulos
    - tests/
      - unit/
      - integration/
      - contract/         # Contract tests entre módulos
    - docs/
      - adrs/
      - api/

# 2. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO
code_standards:
  language: "TypeScript"
  style_guide: "Airbnb Base + Custom Rules"
  
  naming_conventions:
    interfaces: "IPascalCase"
    classes: "PascalCase"
    variables: "camelCase"
    constants: "UPPER_SNAKE_CASE"
    private_members: "_prefixWithUnderscore"
    
  file_structure:
    one_class_per_file: true
    max_file_size: "400 lines"
    index_files: "Barrel exports only"

# 3. TESTES
testing:
  coverage_requirements:
    unit: 80%
    integration: 70%
    e2e: 50%
    
  test_structure:
    pattern: "Given-When-Then"
    file_naming: "*.spec.ts | *.test.ts"
    location: "Colocated with source or separate /tests"
    
  contract_tests:
    required: true
    tools: ["Pact", "Custom Contract Validator"]
    run_on: "PR and nightly"

# 4. COMMITS E VERSIONAMENTO
versioning:
  semver: true
  commit_convention: "Conventional Commits"
  
  commit_types:
    - feat: "New feature"
    - fix: "Bug fix"
    - docs: "Documentation"
    - style: "Formatting"
    - refactor: "Code restructuring"
    - test: "Tests"
    - chore: "Maintenance"
    
  branch_strategy: "GitHub Flow"
  protected_branches: ["main", "develop"]

# 5. DEPENDÊNCIAS
dependencies:
  approval_required: true
  security_scan: "Snyk + Dependabot"
  license_check: "OSI Approved only"
  update_policy: "Monthly minor, Quarterly major"
  
  core_stack:
    runtime: "Node.js 18+"
    framework: "NestJS"
    database: "PostgreSQL 14+"
    cache: "Redis 7+"
    queue: "BullMQ"
    monitoring: "OpenTelemetry + Grafana"

# 6. API DESIGN
api:
  style: "RESTful + RPC for internal"
  versioning: "URL path (/api/v1/)"
  documentation: "OpenAPI 3.0"
  pagination: "Cursor-based"
  rate_limiting: "Per user + IP"
  
  response_format:
    success: "{ data: T, meta?: Metadata }"
    error: "{ error: { code: string, message: string, details?: any } }"

# 7. SEGURANÇA
security:
  authentication: "JWT + Refresh Tokens"
  authorization: "RBAC + ABAC"
  encryption: "AES-256 for data at rest"
  hashing: "Argon2 for passwords"
  headers: "Helmet.js defaults + CSP"
  audit_logging: "All mutations logged"

# 8. PERFORMANCE
performance:
  query_timeout: "5s"
  response_time_sla: "200ms p95"
  payload_limit: "10MB"
  compression: "Brotli for >1KB"
  caching_strategy: "CDN + Redis layers"
```

## 3. Plano de Migração V9 → V10

```javascript
// migration-plan.js
/**
 * PLANO DE MIGRAÇÃO INCREMENTAL - MODO HIVE
 * Estratégia: Strangler Fig Pattern + Parallel Run
 */

module.exports = {
  // FASE 1: PREPARAÇÃO (Sprint 1-2)
  phase1: {
    name: "Foundation & Tooling",
    duration: "4 weeks",
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "MIG-001",
        description: "Setup monorepo com Lerna/Turborepo",
        owner: "Infra",
        acceptance: [
          "Build pipeline funcionando",
          "Dependencies isoladas por módulo",
          "Hot reload entre módulos"
        ]
      },
      {
        id: "MIG-002",
        description: "CI/CD pipeline para módulos",
        owner: "DevOps",
        acceptance: [
          "Deploy independente por módulo (feature flag)",
          "Rollback automático em 5min",
          "Health checks por módulo"
        ]
      },
      {
        id: "MIG-003",
        description: "Observabilidade distribuída",
        owner: "SRE",
        acceptance: [
          "Tracing entre módulos (OpenTelemetry)",
          "Metrics por módulo no Grafana",
          "Log aggregation com correlation IDs"
        ]
      }
    ],
    success_metrics: {
      build_time: "< 10min",
      test_coverage: "> 70%",
      deployment_frequency: "Daily"
    }
  },

  // FASE 2: MÓDULO PILOTO (Sprint 3-4)
  phase2: {
    name: "Auth Module Strangulation",
    duration: "6 weeks",
    target_module: "Authentication",
    strategy: "Parallel Run with Proxy",
    
    steps: [
      {
        step: "1. Create Module Boundary",
        action: "Extract auth domain to /modules/auth",
        validation: "Contract tests with V9"
      },
      {
        step: "2. Implement New Module",
        action: "Build V10 auth with new standards",
        validation: "100% test coverage, security audit"
      },
      {
        step: "3. Deploy Side-by-Side",
        action: "Run V9 and V10 auth simultaneously",
        validation: "Traffic split 1%/99% (V10/V9)"
      },
      {
        step: "4. Proxy Layer Routing",
        action: "API Gateway routes to appropriate version",
        validation: "Zero downtime, session persistence"
      },
      {
        step: "5. Gradual Traffic Shift",
        action: "Increase V10 traffic 10% weekly",
        validation: "Monitor errors, latency, business metrics"
      },
      {
        step: "6. Decommission V9",
        action: "Redirect 100% traffic, remove V9 code",
        validation: "30 days monitoring, then archive"
      }
    ],
    
    rollback_plan: {
      trigger: "Error rate > 1% OR latency increase > 50%",
      action: "Revert traffic to V9 in < 5min",
      notification: "Auto-alert to #prod-incidents"
    }
  },

  // FASE 3: MIGRAÇÃO EM PARALELO (Sprint 5-10)
  phase3: {
    name: "Parallel Module Migration",
    duration: "12 weeks",
    mode: "Hive Mode - 3 squads in parallel",
    
    squads: [
      {
        name: "Hive Alpha",
        modules: ["User Management", "Profile"],
        dependencies: ["Auth (completed)"],
        start_week: 5,
        duration: "6 weeks"
      },
      {
        name: "Hive Beta", 
        modules: ["Content", "Media Storage"],
        dependencies: ["Auth"],
        start_week: 7,
        duration: "8 weeks"
      },
      {
        name: "Hive Gamma",
        modules: ["Notifications", "Messaging"],
        dependencies: ["Auth", "User Management"],
        start_week: 9,
        duration: "6 weeks"
      }
    ],
    
    coordination: {
      sync_frequency: "Daily standup + Weekly architecture review",
      conflict_resolution: "Tech Lead arbitration",
      integration_testing: "Nightly full-stack tests"
    }
  },

  // FASE 4: CONSOLIDAÇÃO (Sprint 11-12)
  phase4: {
    name: "Integration & Optimization",
    duration: "4 weeks",
    tasks: [
      {
        task: "Cross-module transactions",
        solution: "Saga Pattern with compensation",
        tools: ["BullMQ for orchestration"]
      },
      {
        task: "Shared cache layer",
        solution: "Redis cluster with namespace per module",
        validation: "Cache hit ratio > 80%"
      },
      {
        task: "Unified API Gateway",
        solution: "Kong with plugin per module",
        features: ["Rate limiting", "Authentication", "Request transformation"]
      },
      {
        task: "Performance benchmarking",
        metrics: [
          "p95 latency < 200ms",
          "Throughput > 1000 req/sec",
          "Error rate < 0.1%"
        ]
      }
    ]
  },

  // METRICS & MONITORING
  metrics: {
    business: [
      "User retention during migration > 99%",
      "Zero revenue impact",
      "Support tickets unchanged"
    ],
    technical: [
      "Performance: Latency variance < 20%",
      "Reliability: Availability > 99.95%",
      "Quality: Bug rate reduction > 40%"
    ],
    team: [
      "Deployment frequency increase 2x",
      "Lead time for changes reduction 50%",
      "Change failure rate < 5%"
    ]
  },

  // RISK REGISTER
  risks: [
    {
      id: "RISK-001",
      description: "Database schema conflicts during parallel migration",
      probability: "Medium",
      impact: "High",
      mitigation: [
        "Database per module with shared views",
        "Schema change coordination process",
        "Backup every 4 hours during migration"
      ],
      owner: "Tech Lead"
    },
    {
      id: "RISK-002",
      description: "Inconsistent state between V9 and V10 modules",
      probability: "Low",
      impact: "High", 
      mitigation: [
        "Dual-write with reconciliation job",
        "State comparison dashboard",
        "Automatic rollback on divergence"
      ],
      owner: "SRE"
    },
    {
      id: "RISK-003",
      description: "Team velocity drop due to context switching",
      probability: "High",
      impact: "Medium",
      mitigation: [
        "Dedicated migration squads",
        "Pair programming between V9/V10 experts",
        "Weekly knowledge transfer sessions"
      ],
      owner: "Squad Leader"
    }
  ]
};
```

## 4. Template de Módulo V10

```typescript
// modules/template/README.md
# MODULE TEMPLATE - V10 ARCHITECTURE

## Structure
```
modules/{module-name}/
├── domain/           # Business logic (framework-agnostic)
│   ├── entities/     # Domain objects
│   ├── value-objects/# Immutable values  
│   ├── aggregates/   # Transaction boundaries
│   ├── repositories/ # Interface definitions
│   └── services/     # Domain services
├── application/      # Use cases
│   ├── use-cases/    # Command/Query handlers
│   ├── dtos/         # Data transfer objects
│   └── interfaces/   # Application contracts
├── infrastructure/   # Framework implementations
│   ├── persistence/  # Repository implementations
│   ├── external/     # External service clients
│   ├── messaging/    # Event publishers/consumers
│   └── cache/        # Caching implementations
├── presentation/     # Delivery mechanisms
│   ├── controllers/  # REST/GraphQL endpoints
│   ├── queues/       # Job handlers
│   └── sockets/      # WebSocket handlers
├── tests/           # All test types
│   ├── unit/        # Domain/Application tests
│   ├── integration/ # Infrastructure tests
│   └── contract/    # Contract tests
└── index.ts         # Module exports
```

// modules/template/domain/entities/user.entity.ts
/**
 * DOMAIN ENTITY - Business rules only
 * No framework dependencies
 */
export interface UserProps {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  name: string;
  status: UserStatus;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

export enum UserStatus {
  ACTIVE = 'ACTIVE',
  INACTIVE = 'INACTIVE',
  SUSPENDED = 'SUSPENDED'
}

export class User {
  constructor(private readonly props: UserProps) {}
  
  // Business methods
  activate(): void {
    if (this.props.status === UserStatus.SUSPENDED) {
      throw new Error('Suspended users cannot be activated');
    }
    this.props.status = UserStatus.ACTIVE;
    this.props.updatedAt = new Date();
  }
  
  // Getters only - mutation via methods
  get id(): string { return this.props.id; }
  get email(): string { return this.props.email; }
  // ... other getters
}

// modules/template/application/use-cases/create-user.use-case.ts
/**
 * USE CASE - Application business logic
 * Orchestrates domain objects and infrastructure
 */
export interface CreateUserCommand {
  email: string;
  name: string;
  password: string;
}

export interface CreateUserResult {
  userId: string;
  activationToken: string;
}

export class CreateUserUseCase {
  constructor(
    private readonly userRepository: IUserRepository,
    private readonly passwordService: IPasswordService,
    private readonly eventPublisher: IEventPublisher
  ) {}
  
  async execute(command: CreateUserCommand): Promise<CreateUserResult> {
    // Validation
    if (!this.isValidEmail(command.email)) {
      throw new ValidationError('Invalid email format');
    }
    
    // Check uniqueness
    const existing = await this.userRepository.findByEmail(command.email);
    if (existing) {
      throw new ConflictError('Email already registered');
    }
    
    // Create domain entity
    const hashedPassword = await this.passwordService.hash(command.password);
    const user = new User({
      id: generateId(),
      email: command.email,
      name: command.name,
      status: UserStatus.INACTIVE,
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
    
    // Persist
    await this.userRepository.save(user);
    
    // Publish domain event
    await this.eventPublisher.publish(new UserCreatedEvent({
      userId: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      timestamp: new Date()
    }));
    
    return {
      userId: user.id,
      activationToken: generateActivationToken(user.id)
    };
  }
  
  private isValidEmail(email: string): boolean {
    return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email);
  }
}

// modules/template/infrastructure/persistence/user.repository.ts
/**
 * REPOSITORY IMP

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Design System

Vou criar um sistema de design completo e profissional para o DIYAPP Evolution V10, com foco em UX premium, componentes reutilizáveis e microinterações refinadas.

            color: var(--text-primary);
            background-color: var(--bg-primary);
            transition: background-color var(--transition-base), color var(--transition-base);
        }
        
        .container {
            width: 100%;
            max-width: var(--max-width-2xl);
            margin: 0 auto;
            padding: 0 var(--space-6);
        }
        
        /* Componentes do Design System */
        
        /* Botões */
        .btn {
            display: inline-flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            gap: var(--space-2);
            padding: var(--space-2) var(--space-4);
            font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
            font-weight: var(--font-weight-medium);
            line-height: var(--line-height-tight);
            border-radius: var(--radius-md);
            border: 1px solid transparent;
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: all var(--transition-base);
            text-decoration: none;
            user-select: none;
            white-space: nowrap;
        }
        
        .btn:focus {
            outline: 2px solid var(--color-primary-500);
            outline-offset: 2px;
        }
        
        .btn:disabled {
            opacity: 0.5;
            cursor: not-allowed;
        }
        
        .btn-primary {
            background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            color: white;
        }
        
        .btn-primary:hover:not(:disabled) {
            background-color: var(--color-primary-700);
            transform: translateY(-1px);
            box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
        }
        
        .btn-primary:active:not(:disabled) {
            background-color: var(--color-primary-800);
            transform: translateY(0);
        }
        
        .btn-secondary {
            background-color: var(--color-secondary-600);
            color: white;
        }
        
        .btn-secondary:hover:not(:disabled) {
            background-color: var(--color-secondary-700);
            transform: translateY(-1px);
            box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
        }
        
        .btn-outline {
            background-color: transparent;
            color: var(--color-primary-700);
            border-color: var(--color-primary-300);
        }
        
        .btn-outline:hover:not(:disabled) {
            background-color: var(--color-primary-50);
            border-color: var(--color-primary-500);
        }
        
        .btn-ghost {
            background-color: transparent;
            color: var(--text-secondary);
            border-color: transparent;
        }
        
        .btn-ghost:hover:not(:disabled) {
            background-color: var(--color-neutral-100);

        }

## 3. vite.config.ts

```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite'
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react'
import path from 'path'

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@design-system': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/design-system')
    }
  },
  build: {
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          'react-vendor': ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          'ui-vendor': ['lucide-react', 'clsx', 'date-fns'],
          'design-system': ['@design-system']
        }
      }
    },
    target: 'es2020',
    minify: 'terser',
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: true,
        drop_debugger: true
      }
    }
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000
  }
})
```

### src/design-system/tokens/spacing.ts

```typescript
export const spacing = {
  // Base unit: 4px (0.25rem)
  0: '0',
  1: '0.25rem',  // 4px
  2: '0.5rem',   // 8px
  3: '0.75rem',  // 12px
  4: '1rem',     // 16px
  5: '1.25rem',  // 20px
  6: '1.5rem',   // 24px
  8: '2rem',     // 32px
  10: '2.5rem',  // 40px
  12: '3rem',    // 48px
  16: '4rem',    // 64px
  20: '5rem',    // 80px
  24: '6rem',    // 96px
  32: '8rem',    // 128px
  40: '10rem',   // 160px
  48: '12rem',   // 192px
  56: '14rem',   // 224px
  64: '16rem',   // 256px
} as const;

export const breakpoints = {
  xs: '320px',
  sm: '640px',
  md: '768px',
  lg: '1024px',
  xl: '1280px',
  '2xl': '1536px',
} as const;

export type SpacingToken = keyof typeof spacing;
export type BreakpointToken = keyof typeof breakpoints;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
# Refatoração de APIs para Performance e Estabilidade
# Arquitetura: RESTful + GraphQL com cache Redis, circuit breakers e otimizações

import asyncio
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Union
from uuid import uuid4

import asyncpg
import redis.asyncio as redis
import uvicorn
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Depends, Query, status, BackgroundTasks
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, validator
from slowapi import Limiter, _rate_limit_exceeded_handler
from slowapi.errors import RateLimitExceeded
from slowapi.util import get_remote_address
from starlette.requests import Request
from starlette.responses import Response
from prometheus_fastapi_instrumentator import Instrumentator
import aioredis
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential, retry_if_exception_type
import async_timeout

# ============================================================================
# CONFIGURAÇÃO E INICIALIZAÇÃO
# ============================================================================

# Configuração de logging estruturado
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='{"timestamp": "%(asctime)s", "level": "%(levelname)s", "correlation_id": "%(correlation_id)s", "service": "v10-api", "endpoint": "%(endpoint)s", "duration_ms": %(duration_ms)d, "status": %(status)d, "message": "%(message)s"}',
    handlers=[logging.StreamHandler()]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# Configurações
class Config:
    # Database
    DB_HOST = "localhost"
    DB_PORT = 5432
    DB_NAME = "diyapp_v10"
    DB_USER = "diyapp_user"
    DB_PASSWORD = "secure_password_here"
    DB_POOL_MIN = 5
    DB_POOL_MAX = 20
    
    # Redis Cache
    REDIS_HOST = "localhost"
    REDIS_PORT = 6379
    REDIS_PASSWORD = None
    REDIS_TTL = 300  # 5 minutos default
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    CB_FAILURE_THRESHOLD = 5
    CB_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT = 60
    CB_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION = (HTTPException, asyncpg.PostgresConnectionError)
    
    # Retry Policy
    RETRY_ATTEMPTS = 3
    RETRY_WAIT_MULTIPLIER = 1
    RETRY_WAIT_MAX = 10
    
    # Rate Limiting
    RATE_LIMIT_DEFAULT = "100/minute"
    
    # Performance
    QUERY_TIMEOUT = 30  # segundos
    CACHE_ENABLED = True
    CACHE_STALE_WHILE_REVALIDATE = 60  # segundos

config = Config()

# ============================================================================
# MODELOS DE DADOS (Pydantic)
# ============================================================================

class User(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid4()))
    email: str = Field(..., min_length=3, max_length=255)
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=100)
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    
    @validator('email')
    def validate_email(cls, v):
        if '@' not in v:
            raise ValueError('Invalid email format')
        return v.lower()

class Project(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid4()))
    user_id: str
    title: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=200)
    description: Optional[str] = Field(None, max_length=1000)
    status: str = Field(default="active", regex="^(active|archived|deleted)$")
    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class APIResponse(BaseModel):
    success: bool
    data: Optional[Any] = None
    error: Optional[str] = None
    meta: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    correlation_id: str

class GraphQLRequest(BaseModel):
    query: str
    variables: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    operationName: Optional[str] = None

# ============================================================================
# DEPENDÊNCIAS E CONEXÕES
# ============================================================================

# Pool de conexões PostgreSQL
class Database:
    _pool: Optional[asyncpg.Pool] = None
    
    @classmethod
    async def get_pool(cls) -> asyncpg.Pool:
        if cls._pool is None:
            cls._pool = await asyncpg.create_pool(
                host=config.DB_HOST,
                port=config.DB_PORT,
                database=config.DB_NAME,
                user=config.DB_USER,
                password=config.DB_PASSWORD,
                min_size=config.DB_POOL_MIN,
                max_size=config.DB_POOL_MAX,
                command_timeout=config.QUERY_TIMEOUT
            )
        return cls._pool
    
    @classmethod
    async def close(cls):
        if cls._pool:
            await cls._pool.close()

# Cliente Redis com connection pooling
class RedisCache:
    _client: Optional[redis.Redis] = None
    
    @classmethod
    async def get_client(cls) -> redis.Redis:
        if cls._client is None:
            cls._client = redis.Redis(
                host=config.REDIS_HOST,
                port=config.REDIS_PORT,
                password=config.REDIS_PASSWORD,
                decode_responses=True,
                max_connections=50
            )
        return cls._client
    
    @classmethod
    async def close(cls):
        if cls._client:
            await cls._client.close()

# Rate Limiter
limiter = Limiter(key_func=get_remote_address)

# ============================================================================
# MIDDLEWARE E INSTRUMENTAÇÃO
# ============================================================================

app = FastAPI(
    title="DIYAPP V10 API",
    description="APIs refatoradas para performance com cache Redis e circuit breakers",
    version="10.0.0",
    docs_url="/api/docs",
    redoc_url="/api/redoc"
)

# CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # Em produção, especificar domínios
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Rate Limiting
app.state.limiter = limiter
app.add_exception_handler(RateLimitExceeded, _rate_limit_exempted_handler)

# Prometheus Metrics
Instrumentator().instrument(app).expose(app, endpoint="/api/metrics")

# Middleware de logging e correlation ID
@app.middleware("http")
async def logging_middleware(request: Request, call_next):
    correlation_id = request.headers.get("X-Correlation-ID", str(uuid4()))
    start_time = datetime.utcnow()
    
    # Adiciona correlation ID ao request state
    request.state.correlation_id = correlation_id
    
    # Processa a requisição
    try:
        response = await call_next(request)
        duration = (datetime.utcnow() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000
        
        # Log estruturado
        logger.info(
            f"Request completed",
            extra={
                "correlation_id": correlation_id,
                "endpoint": f"{request.method} {request.url.path}",
                "duration_ms": int(duration),
                "status": response.status_code,
                "user_agent": request.headers.get("user-agent", ""),
                "ip": request.client.host if request.client else None
            }
        )
        
        # Adiciona correlation ID ao header da resposta
        response.headers["X-Correlation-ID"] = correlation_id
        return response
        
    except Exception as e:
        duration = (datetime.utcnow() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000
        logger.error(
            f"Request failed: {str(e)}",
            extra={
                "correlation_id": correlation_id,
                "endpoint": f"{request.method} {request.url.path}",
                "duration_ms": int(duration),
                "status": 500,
                "error": str(e),
                "stack_trace": logging.Formatter().formatException(e.__traceback__)
            },
            exc_info=True
        )
        raise

# ============================================================================
# UTILITÁRIOS DE PERFORMANCE
# ============================================================================

class CacheManager:
    """Gerenciador de cache com estratégia stale-while-revalidate"""
    
    @staticmethod
    async def get_or_set(
        key: str,
        fetch_func,
        ttl: int = config.REDIS_TTL,
        stale_ttl: int = config.CACHE_STALE_WHILE_REVALIDATE
    ) -> Any:
        """Obtém do cache ou executa a função de fetch"""
        if not config.CACHE_ENABLED:
            return await fetch_func()
        
        redis_client = await RedisCache.get_client()
        
        try:
            # Tenta obter do cache
            cached = await redis_client.get(key)
            if cached:
                data = json.loads(cached)
                
                # Verifica se está stale
                cache_info = await redis_client.ttl(key)
                if cache_info < stale_ttl:
                    # Revalida em background
                    asyncio.create_task(CacheManager._revalidate_cache(key, fetch_func, ttl))
                
                return data
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache read failed: {str(e)}")
        
        # Cache miss ou erro - busca direto
        data = await fetch_func()
        
        # Armazena no cache em background
        asyncio.create_task(CacheManager._set_cache(key, data, ttl))
        
        return data
    
    @staticmethod
    async def _set_cache(key: str, data: Any, ttl: int):
        """Armazena dados no cache"""
        try:
            redis_client = await RedisCache.get_client()
            await redis_client.setex(key, ttl, json.dumps(data, default=str))
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Cache write failed: {str(e)}")
    
    @staticmethod
    async def _revalidate_cache(key: str, fetch_func, ttl: int):
        """Revalida cache stale em background"""
        try:
            data = await fetch_func()
            await CacheManager._set_cache(key, data, ttl)
        except Exception:
            pass  # Falha silenciosa na revalidação
    
    @staticmethod
    async def invalidate(pattern: str):
        """Invalida cache por pattern"""
        try:
            redis_client = await RedisCache.get_client()
            keys = await redis_client.keys(pattern)
            if keys:
                await redis_client.delete(*keys)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Cache invalidation failed: {str(e)}")

class QueryOptimizer:
    """Otimizador de queries PostgreSQL"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def build_user_query(
        user_id: Optional[str] = None,
        email: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 100,
        offset: int = 0
    ) -> tuple[str, list]:
        """Constrói query otimizada para users com parametrização"""
        query_parts = ["SELECT id, email, name, created_at, updated_at FROM users WHERE 1=1"]
        params = []
        param_counter = 1
        
        if user_id:
            query_parts.append(f"AND id = ${param_counter}")
            params.append(user_id)
            param_counter += 1
        
        if email:
            query_parts.append(f"AND email = ${param_counter}")
            params.append(email)
            param_counter += 1
        
        query_parts.append(f"ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ${param_counter}")
        params.append(limit)
        param_counter += 1
        
        query_parts.append(f"OFFSET ${param_counter}")
        params.append(offset)
        
        return " ".join(query_parts), params
    
    @staticmethod
    def build_project_query(
        user_id: Optional[str] = None,
        project_id: Optional[str] = None,
        status: Optional[str] = None,
        tags: Optional[List[str]] = None,
        limit: int = 100,
        offset: int = 0
    ) -> tuple[str, list]:
        """Constrói query otimizada para projects com parametrização"""
        query_parts = [
            "SELECT p.id, p.user_id, p.title, p.description, p.status,",
            "p.tags, p.metadata, p.created_at, p.updated_at,",
            "u.email as user_email, u.name as user_name",
            "FROM projects p",
            "LEFT JOIN users u ON p.user_id = u.id",
            "WHERE 1=1"
        ]
        params = []
        param_counter = 1
        
        if user_id:
            query_parts.append(f"AND p.user_id = ${param_counter}")
            params.append(user_id)
            param_counter += 1
        
        if project_id:
            query_parts.append(f"AND p.id = ${param_counter}")
            params.append(project_id)
            param_counter += 1
        
        if status:
            query_parts.append(f"AND p.status = ${param_counter}")
            params.append(status)
            param_counter += 1
        
        if tags:
            # Query para array containment
            query_parts.append(f"AND p.tags @> ${param_counter}")
            params.append(tags)
            param_counter += 1
        
        query_parts.append(f"ORDER BY p.updated_at DESC LIMIT ${param_counter}")
        params.append(limit)
        param_counter += 1
        
        query_parts.append(f"OFFSET ${param_counter}")
        params.append(offset)
        
        return " ".join(query_parts), params

# ============================================================================
# REPOSITÓRIOS COM RESILIÊNCIA
# ============================================================================

class UserRepository:
    """Repository pattern para users com circuit breaker e retry"""
    
    @staticmethod
    @circuit(
        failure_threshold=config.CB_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
        recovery_timeout=config.CB_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
        expected_exception=config.CB_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION
    )
    @retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(config.RETRY_ATTEMPTS),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=config.RETRY_WAIT_MULTIPLIER, max=config.RETRY_WAIT_MAX),
        retry=retry_if_exception_type((asyncpg.PostgresConnectionError,))
    )
    async def get_user_by_id(user_id: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Obtém usuário por ID com resiliência"""
        pool = await Database.get_pool()
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            # QUERY PARAMETRIZADA - ZERO SQL INJECTION
            query = "SELECT id, email, name, created_at, updated_at FROM users WHERE id = $1"
            row = await conn.fetchrow(query, user_id)
            return dict(row) if row else None
    
    @staticmethod
    @circuit(
        failure_threshold=config.CB_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
        recovery_timeout=config.CB_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
        expected_exception=config.CB_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION
    )
    async def create_user(user_data: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Cria novo usuário"""
        pool = await Database.get_pool()
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            # QUERY PARAMETRIZADA
            query = """
                INSERT INTO users (id, email, name, created_at, updated_at)
                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)
                RETURNING id, email, name, created_at, updated_at
            """
            row = await conn.fetchrow(
                query,
                user_data["id"],
                user_data["email"],
                user_data["name"],
                user_data["created_at"],
                user_data["updated_at"]
            )
            return dict(row)
    
    @staticmethod
    async def search_users(
        email: Optional[str] = None,
        name: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 100,
        offset: int = 0
    ) -> List[Dict]:
        """Busca usuários com query otimizada"""
        pool = await Database.get_pool()
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            query, params = QueryOptimizer.build_user_query(
                email=email,
                limit=limit,
                offset=offset
            )
            rows = await conn.fetch(query, *params)
            return [dict(row) for row in rows]

class ProjectRepository:
    """Repository pattern para projects com otimizações"""
    
    @staticmethod
    @circuit(
        failure_threshold=config.CB_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
        recovery_timeout=config.CB_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
        expected_exception=config.CB_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION
    )
    @retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(config.RETRY_ATTEMPTS),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=config.RETRY_WAIT_MULTIPLIER, max=config.RETRY_WAIT_MAX),
        retry=retry_if_exception_type((asyncpg.PostgresConnectionError,))
    )
    async def get_project_by_id(project_id: str, user_id: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Obtém projeto por ID com join otimizado"""
        pool = await Database.get_pool()
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            if user_id:
                # QUERY PARAMETRIZADA COM JOIN
                query = """
                    SELECT p.id, p.user_id, p.title, p.description, p.status,
                           p.tags, p.metadata, p.created_at, p.updated_at,
                           u.email as user_email, u.name as user_name

## 1. Terraform Configuration

### `terraform/providers.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }

  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v10/production/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
  }
}
```

### `terraform/main.tf`
```hcl
# Data sources
data "aws_availability_zones" "available" {
  state = "available"
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "cluster" {
  name = module.eks.cluster_name
}

# VPC Module
module "vpc" {
  source = "./modules/vpc"

  name                 = "${var.cluster_name}-vpc"
  cidr                 = var.vpc_cidr
  azs                  = var.availability_zones
  private_subnets      = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets       = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
  enable_nat_gateway   = true
  single_nat_gateway   = false
  enable_dns_hostnames = true

  tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
  }

  public_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
  }

  private_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
  }
}

# EKS Module
module "eks" {
  source = "./modules/eks"

  cluster_name    = var.cluster_name
  cluster_version = "1.28"

  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnets

  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    diyapp = {
      min_size     = var.min_node_count
      max_size     = var.max_node_count
      desired_size = var.min_node_count

      instance_types = [var.node_instance_type]

      capacity_type = "ON_DEMAND"

      labels = {
        role = "diyapp"
      }

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"             = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
  }
}

  source = "./modules/monitoring"

  cluster_name       = module.eks.cluster_name
  cluster_endpoint   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_data    = module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data

  slo_llm_latency_p95 = var.slo_llm_latency_p95

  environment        = var.environment
}

  version = "~> 5.0"

  create_role                   = true
  role_name                     = "diyapp-eks-admin"
  provider_url                  = module.eks.oidc_provider
  role_policy_arns              = ["arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AdministratorAccess"]
  oidc_fully_qualified_subjects = ["system:serviceaccount:kube-system:aws-node"]
}

# Outputs

  description = "Kubernetes Cluster Name"

}

### `kubernetes/deployments/diyapp-api.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v10
    component: api
spec:
  replicas: 3
  revisionHistoryLimit: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v10
        component: api
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "3000"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: diyapp-service-account
      containers:
      - name: diyapp-api
        image: diyapp/api:v10.0.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        - containerPort: 3001
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          value: "info"
        - name: PORT
          value: "3000"
        - name: METRICS_PORT
          value: "3001"
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "1Gi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 1
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /startup
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 30
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config
          mountPath: /app/config
      volumes:
      - name: config
        configMap:
          name: diyapp-config
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 100
            podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - diyapp-api
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      tolerations:
      - key: "node.kubernetes.io/unreachable"
        operator: "Exists"
        effect: "NoExecute"
        tolerationSeconds: 300
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: diyapp-service-account
  namespace: diyapp
  annotations:
    eks.amazonaws.com/role-arn: arn:aws:iam::${AWS_ACCOUNT_ID}:role/diyapp-eks-admin
```

## 1. docker-compose.yml - Infraestrutura Data Warehouse

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Data Warehouse
  postgres-dw:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_data_warehouse
      POSTGRES_USER: data_engineer
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DW_PASSWORD:-secure_password_123}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init_warehouse.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U data_engineer"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Airflow para orquestração
  airflow-webserver:
    build: ./airflow
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__CORE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres-airflow/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./dbt:/opt/airflow/dbt
      - ./logs:/opt/airflow/logs
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    depends_on:
      postgres-airflow:
        condition: service_healthy
    command: webserver

  postgres-airflow:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: airflow
      POSTGRES_USER: airflow
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: airflow
    volumes:
      - postgres_airflow_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  # Metabase para visualização
  metabase:
    image: metabase/metabase:latest
    environment:
      MB_DB_TYPE: postgres
      MB_DB_DBNAME: metabase
      MB_DB_PORT: 5432
      MB_DB_HOST: postgres-metabase
      MB_DB_USER: metabase
      MB_DB_PASS: metabase
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      postgres-metabase:
        condition: service_healthy

  postgres-metabase:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: metabase
      POSTGRES_USER: metabase
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: metabase
    volumes:
      - postgres_metabase_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  # API para ingestão de dados
  data-ingestion-api:
    build: ./src
    environment:
      DW_CONNECTION_STRING: postgresql://data_engineer:secure_password_123@postgres-dw:5432/diyapp_data_warehouse
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    depends_on:
      postgres-dw:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./src:/app

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  postgres_airflow_data:
  postgres_metabase_data:

        tests:
          - not_null

        description: "Indicador de sucesso"
        tests:
          - not_null

        description: "Feature que gerou a chamada"
        tests:
          - not_null

  - name: stg_users
    description: "Usuários limpos e padronizados"

      - name: user_id
        description: "ID único do usuário"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null

## 4. dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql - Transformação de Eventos

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        TIMESTAMP 'epoch' + (event_timestamp / 1000) * INTERVAL '1 second' AS event_timestamp,
        feature_name,
        session_id,
        properties::jsonb AS properties,
        ingested_at
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND user_id IS NOT NULL
      AND event_type IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    event_timestamp,
    feature_name,
    session_id,
    properties,
    ingested_at,
    DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
    EXTRACT(HOUR FROM event_timestamp) AS event_hour
FROM raw_events
```

## 5. dbt/models/marts/mart_product/daily_active_users.sql - Métrica de DAU

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='marts_product',
        tags=['daily', 'product_metrics']
    )
}}

WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS daily_sessions,
        COUNT(*) AS daily_events
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

daily_activity AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS daily_active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN daily_events >= 3 THEN user_id END) AS engaged_users,
        AVG(daily_sessions) AS avg_sessions_per_user,
        AVG(daily_events) AS avg_events_per_user,
        SUM(daily_events) AS total_daily_events
    FROM daily_events
    GROUP BY 1
),

rolling_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        daily_active_users,
        engaged_users,
        avg_sessions_per_user,
        avg_events_per_user,
        total_daily_events,
        AVG(daily_active_users) OVER (
            ORDER BY event_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_avg_dau,
        AVG(engaged_users) OVER (
            ORDER BY event_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_avg_engaged_users
    FROM daily_activity
)

SELECT
    event_date,
    daily_active_users,
    engaged_users,
    avg_sessions_per_user,
    avg_events_per_user,
    total_daily_events,
    weekly_avg_dau,
    weekly_avg_engaged_users,
    CASE 
        WHEN daily_active_users < weekly_avg_dau * 0.8 THEN 'ALERT: DAU abaixo do esperado'
        WHEN daily_active_users > weekly_avg_dau * 1.2 THEN 'ALERT: DAU acima do esperado'
        ELSE 'NORMAL'
    END AS dau_health_status
FROM rolling_metrics
ORDER BY event_date DESC
```

## 6. dbt/models/marts/mart_ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql - Custo LLM por Feature

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='marts_ai',
        tags=['hourly', 'llm_metrics', 'cost']
    )
}}

WITH hourly_costs AS (
    SELECT
        DATE_TRUNC('hour', ingested_at) AS hour_bucket,
        feature_name,
        provider,
        model,
        COUNT(*) AS total_calls,
        SUM(prompt_tokens) AS total_prompt_tokens,
        SUM(completion_tokens) AS total_completion_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS successful_calls,
        COUNT(*) - SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS failed_calls
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE ingested_at >= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP - INTERVAL '7 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

feature_daily_summary AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(hour_bucket) AS cost_date,
        feature_name,
        provider,
        model,
        SUM(total_calls) AS daily_calls,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS daily_tokens,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) AS daily_cost_usd,
        AVG(avg_latency_ms) AS daily_avg_latency,
        SUM(successful_calls) AS daily_successful_calls,
        SUM(failed_calls) AS daily_failed_calls,
        CASE 
            WHEN SUM(total_calls) > 0 
            THEN SUM(successful_calls)::DECIMAL / SUM(total_calls) 
            ELSE 0 
        END AS daily_success_rate
    FROM hourly_costs
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

cost_anomalies AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        AVG(daily_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, provider, model 
            ORDER BY cost_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_avg_cost,
        STDDEV(daily_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, provider, model 
            ORDER BY cost_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_std_cost
    FROM feature_daily_summary
)

SELECT
    cost_date,
    feature_name,
    provider,
    model,
    daily_calls,
    daily_tokens,
    daily_cost_usd,
    daily_avg_latency,
    daily_successful_calls,
    daily_failed_calls,
    daily_success_rate,
    weekly_avg_cost,
    weekly_std_cost,
    CASE 
        WHEN daily_cost_usd > weekly_avg_cost + (3 * weekly_std_cost) 
             AND weekly_std_cost > 0 
        THEN 'ALERT: Custo acima de 3σ'
        WHEN daily_success_rate < 0.95 
        THEN 'ALERT: Success rate abaixo de 95%'
        WHEN daily_avg_latency > 5000 
        THEN 'AL

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Auto-scaling, Anomaly Detection e Rollback Automático

Vou implementar um sistema completo de auto-scaling, detecção de anomalias e rollback automático para garantir estabilidade 100% autônoma.

## Estrutura do Sistema

```
src/
├── monitoring/
│   ├── anomaly-detector.js
│   ├── metrics-collector.js
│   └── health-check.js
├── scaling/
│   ├── auto-scaler.js
│   ├── scaling-policies.js
│   └── resource-manager.js
├── deployment/
│   ├── rollback-manager.js
│   ├── version-control.js
│   └── deployment-strategies.js
├── config/
│   └── scaling-config.js
├── database/
│   └── metrics-db.js
└── api/
    └── monitoring-api.js
```

## 1. Configuração Principal (scaling-config.js)

```javascript
// src/config/scaling-config.js
module.exports = {
  // Configurações de Auto-scaling
  autoScaling: {
    enabled: true,
    checkInterval: 30000, // 30 segundos
    cooldownPeriod: 300000, // 5 minutos
    scaleUpThreshold: 80, // 80% de utilização
    scaleDownThreshold: 30, // 30% de utilização
    maxInstances: 10,
    minInstances: 2,
    scaleUpIncrement: 2,
    scaleDownIncrement: 1
  },

  // Configurações de Anomaly Detection
  anomalyDetection: {
    enabled: true,
    checkInterval: 60000, // 1 minuto
    metrics: {
      cpu: {
        threshold: 90,
        duration: 300000, // 5 minutos acima do threshold
        anomalyScore: 0.8
      },
      memory: {
        threshold: 85,
        duration: 300000,
        anomalyScore: 0.7
      },
      responseTime: {
        threshold: 2000, // 2 segundos
        duration: 180000, // 3 minutos
        anomalyScore: 0.9
      },
      errorRate: {
        threshold: 5, // 5%
        duration: 120000, // 2 minutos
        anomalyScore: 1.0
      }
    },
    rollingWindow: 15, // minutos para análise histórica
    anomalyThreshold: 0.75 // score mínimo para considerar anomalia
  },

  // Configurações de Rollback Automático
  autoRollback: {
    enabled: true,
    healthCheckInterval: 10000, // 10 segundos
    failureThreshold: 3, // 3 falhas consecutivas
    rollbackWindow: 900000, // 15 minutos
    maxRollbackVersions: 3,
    versionHistorySize: 10
  },

  // Notificações
  notifications: {
    enabled: true,
    providers: ['slack', 'email'],
    slackWebhook: process.env.SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL,
    emailRecipients: process.env.EMAIL_RECIPIENTS?.split(',') || []
  }
};
```

## 2. Coletor de Métricas (metrics-collector.js)

```javascript
// src/monitoring/metrics-collector.js
const os = require('os');
const EventEmitter = require('events');

class MetricsCollector extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config) {
    super();
    this.config = config;
    this.metricsHistory = [];
    this.maxHistorySize = 1000;
    this.collectionInterval = 10000; // 10 segundos
  }

  async start() {
    console.log('🚀 Iniciando coletor de métricas...');
    setInterval(() => this.collectMetrics(), this.collectionInterval);
    this.collectMetrics(); // Coleta inicial
  }

  async collectMetrics() {
    try {
      const metrics = {
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        cpu: await this.getCpuUsage(),
        memory: this.getMemoryUsage(),
        network: this.getNetworkStats(),
        system: this.getSystemMetrics(),
        application: await this.getApplicationMetrics()
      };

      this.metricsHistory.push(metrics);
      
      // Mantém histórico limitado
      if (this.metricsHistory.length > this.maxHistorySize) {
        this.metricsHistory = this.metricsHistory.slice(-this.maxHistorySize);
      }

      this.emit('metrics-collected', metrics);
      return metrics;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Erro ao coletar métricas:', error);
      this.emit('metrics-error', error);
    }
  }

  async getCpuUsage() {
    const startMeasure = this.cpuAverage();
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
    const endMeasure = this.cpuAverage();
    
    const idleDifference = endMeasure.idle - startMeasure.idle;
    const totalDifference = endMeasure.total - startMeasure.total;
    
    return {
      usage: 100 - (100 * idleDifference / totalDifference),
      cores: os.cpus().length,
      load: os.loadavg()
    };
  }

  cpuAverage() {
    const cpus = os.cpus();
    let idle = 0;
    let total = 0;
    
    cpus.forEach(cpu => {
      for (const type in cpu.times) {
        total += cpu.times[type];
      }
      idle += cpu.times.idle;
    });
    
    return { idle, total };
  }

  getMemoryUsage() {
    const total = os.totalmem();
    const free = os.freemem();
    const used = total - free;
    
    return {
      total: this.bytesToGB(total),
      used: this.bytesToGB(used),
      free: this.bytesToGB(free),
      usage: (used / total) * 100
    };
  }

  getNetworkStats() {
    const interfaces = os.networkInterfaces();
    const stats = {};
    
    Object.keys(interfaces).forEach(iface => {
      stats[iface] = interfaces[iface].map(info => ({
        address: info.address,
        netmask: info.netmask,
        family: info.family,
        mac: info.mac,
        internal: info.internal
      }));
    });
    
    return stats;
  }

  getSystemMetrics() {
    return {
      uptime: os.uptime(),
      platform: os.platform(),
      arch: os.arch(),
      hostname: os.hostname(),
      userInfo: os.userInfo()
    };
  }

  async getApplicationMetrics() {
    // Métricas específicas da aplicação
    const memoryUsage = process.memoryUsage();
    
    return {
      processMemory: {
        rss: this.bytesToMB(memoryUsage.rss),
        heapTotal: this.bytesToMB(memoryUsage.heapTotal),
        heapUsed: this.bytesToMB(memoryUsage.heapUsed),
        external: this.bytesToMB(memoryUsage.external)
      },
      node: {
        version: process.version,
        pid: process.pid,
        uptime: process.uptime()
      }
    };
  }

  bytesToGB(bytes) {
    return bytes / 1024 / 1024 / 1024;
  }

  bytesToMB(bytes) {
    return bytes / 1024 / 1024;
  }

  getHistoricalMetrics(minutes = 15) {
    const cutoff = Date.now() - (minutes * 60 * 1000);
    return this.metricsHistory.filter(m => m.timestamp >= cutoff);
  }

  getCurrentMetrics() {
    return this.metricsHistory[this.metricsHistory.length - 1] || null;
  }
}

module.exports = MetricsCollector;
```

## 3. Detector de Anomalias (anomaly-detector.js)

```javascript
// src/monitoring/anomaly-detector.js
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const { MLAnomalyDetector } = require('./ml-detector');

class AnomalyDetector extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config, metricsCollector) {
    super();
    this.config = config.anomalyDetection;
    this.metricsCollector = metricsCollector;
    this.anomalies = [];
    this.mlDetector = new MLAnomalyDetector();
    this.checkInterval = null;
  }

  async start() {
    console.log('🔍 Iniciando detector de anomalias...');
    
    // Treina modelo ML com dados históricos
    await this.mlDetector.train(this.metricsCollector.getHistoricalMetrics(60));
    
    // Escuta por novas métricas
    this.metricsCollector.on('metrics-collected', (metrics) => {
      this.analyzeMetrics(metrics);
    });
    
    // Verificação periódica
    this.checkInterval = setInterval(
      () => this.periodicCheck(),
      this.config.checkInterval
    );
  }

  async analyzeMetrics(metrics) {
    try {
      const anomalies = [];
      
      // Verificação baseada em regras
      const ruleBasedAnomalies = this.checkRuleBased(metrics);
      anomalies.push(...ruleBasedAnomalies);
      
      // Verificação baseada em ML
      const mlAnomalies = await this.mlDetector.detect(metrics);
      anomalies.push(...mlAnomalies);
      
      // Consolida anomalias
      const consolidatedAnomalies = this.consolidateAnomalies(anomalies);
      
      if (consolidatedAnomalies.length > 0) {
        this.handleAnomalies(consolidatedAnomalies, metrics);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Erro na análise de anomalias:', error);
    }
  }

  checkRuleBased(metrics) {
    const anomalies = [];
    const rules = this.config.metrics;
    
    // CPU
    if (metrics.cpu.usage > rules.cpu.threshold) {
      anomalies.push({
        type: 'cpu',
        severity: 'high',
        value: metrics.cpu.usage,
        threshold: rules.cpu.threshold,
        score: rules.cpu.anomalyScore
      });
    }
    
    // Memória
    if (metrics.memory.usage > rules.memory.threshold) {
      anomalies.push({
        type: 'memory',
        severity: 'high',
        value: metrics.memory.usage,
        threshold: rules.memory.threshold,
        score: rules.memory.anomalyScore
      });
    }
    
    // Verifica tendências
    const historical = this.metricsCollector.getHistoricalMetrics(5); // 5 minutos
    if (historical.length > 10) {
      const cpuTrend = this.calculateTrend(historical.map(m => m.cpu.usage));
      if (cpuTrend > 20) { // Aumento de 20% nos últimos 5 minutos
        anomalies.push({
          type: 'cpu_trend',
          severity: 'medium',
          trend: cpuTrend,
          score: 0.6
        });
      }
    }
    
    return anomalies;
  }

  calculateTrend(values) {
    if (values.length < 2) return 0;
    
    const first = values[0];
    const last = values[values.length - 1];
    return ((last - first) / first) * 100;
  }

  consolidateAnomalies(anomalies) {
    const consolidated = [];
    const anomalyMap = new Map();
    
    anomalies.forEach(anomaly => {
      const key = `${anomaly.type}_${anomaly.severity}`;
      if (!anomalyMap.has(key)) {
        anomalyMap.set(key, {
          ...anomaly,
          count: 1,
          firstSeen: Date.now(),
          lastSeen: Date.now()
        });
      } else {
        const existing = anomalyMap.get(key);
        existing.count++;
        existing.lastSeen = Date.now();
        existing.score = Math.max(existing.score, anomaly.score);
      }
    });
    
    anomalyMap.forEach(anomaly => {
      if (anomaly.score >= this.config.anomalyThreshold) {
        consolidated.push(anomaly);
      }
    });
    
    return consolidated;
  }

  async handleAnomalies(anomalies, metrics) {
    const criticalAnomalies = anomalies.filter(a => a.severity === 'high' || a.score > 0.8);
    
    if (criticalAnomalies.length > 0) {
      console.warn('🚨 Anomalias críticas detectadas:', criticalAnomalies);
      
      // Emite evento para ações corretivas
      this.emit('critical-anomaly', {
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        anomalies: criticalAnomalies,
        metrics: metrics,
        requiresAction: true
      });
      
      // Notifica equipe
      await this.notifyTeam(criticalAnomalies, metrics);
    }
    
    // Armazena todas as anomalias
    this.anomalies.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      anomalies: anomalies,
      metrics: metrics
    });
    
    // Limita histórico
    if (this.anomalies.length > 1000) {
      this.anomalies = this.anomalies.slice(-1000);
    }
  }

  async notifyTeam(anomalies, metrics) {
    const message = {
      text: '🚨 *ANOMALIAS CRÍTICAS DETECTADAS*',
      attachments: anomalies.map(anomaly => ({
        color: anomaly.severity === 'high' ? '#ff0000' : '#ff9900',
        fields: [
          { title: 'Tipo', value: anomaly.type, short: true },
          { title: 'Severidade', value: anomaly.severity, short: true },
          { title: 'Valor', value: anomaly.value?.toFixed(2) || 'N/A', short: true },
          { title: 'Score', value: anomaly.score.toFixed(2), short: true }
        ],
        ts: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
      }))
    };
    
    // Implementar notificação via Slack/Email
    console.log('Notificação enviada:', message);
  }

  async periodicCheck() {
    // Verifica anomalias persistentes
    const recentAnomalies = this.anomalies.filter(
      a => Date.now() - a.timestamp < this.config.metrics.cpu.duration
    );
    
    if (recentAnomalies.length > 5) {
      console.warn('⚠️ Múltiplas anomalias detectadas em curto período');
      this.emit('anomaly-pattern', recentAnomalies);
    }
  }

  stop() {
    if (this.checkInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.checkInterval);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = AnomalyDetector;
```

## 4. Detector ML (ml-detector.js)

```javascript
// src/monitoring/ml-detector.js
const tf = require('@tensorflow/tfjs-node');

class MLAnomalyDetector {
  constructor() {
    this.model = null;
    this.isTrained = false;
    this.threshold = 0.1;
  }

  async train(historicalData) {
    if (historicalData.length < 50) {
      console.warn('Dados insuficientes para treinamento ML');
      return;
    }

    console.log('🤖 Treinando modelo de detecção de anomalias...');
    
    // Prepara dados para treinamento
    const features = this.extractFeatures(historicalData);
    
    // Cria e treina modelo autoencoder
    this.model = this.createAutoencoder(features[0].length);
    
    await this.model.fit(
      tf.tensor2d(features),
      tf.tensor2d(features),
      {
        epochs: 100,
        batchSize: 32,
        validationSplit: 0.2,
        verbose: 0
      }
    );
    
    this.isTrained = true;
    console.log('✅ Modelo ML treinado com sucesso');
  }

  extractFeatures(data) {
    return data.map(metrics => [
      metrics.cpu.usage / 100,
      metrics.memory.usage / 100,
      metrics.application.processMemory.heapUsed / 1024, // Normaliza
      metrics.application.processMemory.rss / 1024
    ]);
  }

  createAutoencoder(inputDim) {
    const model = tf.sequential();
    
    // Encoder
    model.add(tf.layers.dense({
      units: Math.floor(inputDim / 2),
      activation: 'relu',
      inputShape: [inputDim]
    }));
    
    model.add(tf.layers.dense({
      units: Math.floor(inputDim / 4),
      activation: 'relu'
    }));
    
    // Decoder
    model.add(tf.layers.dense({
      units: Math.floor(inputDim / 2),
      activation: 'relu'
    }));
    
    model.add(tf.layers.dense({
      units: inputDim,
      activation: 'sigmoid'
    }));
    
    model.compile({
      optimizer: 'adam',
      loss: 'meanSquaredError'
    });
    
    return model;
  }

  async detect(metrics) {
    if (!this.isTrained || !this.model) {
      return [];
    }

    try {
      const features = this.extractFeatures([metrics]);
      const input = tf.tensor2d(features);
      
      // Predição
      const reconstruction = this.model.predict(input);
      
      // Calcula erro de reconstrução
      const error = tf.losses.meanSquaredError(input, reconstruction);
      const errorValue = (await error.dataSync())[0];
      
      input.dispose();
      reconstruction.dispose();
      error.dispose();
      
      // Se erro for alto, é uma anomalia
      if (errorValue > this.threshold) {
        return [{
          type: 'ml_anomaly',
          severity: 'medium',
          score: Math.min(errorValue * 10, 1.0), // Normaliza para 0-1
          reconstructionError: errorValue
        }];
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Erro na detecção ML:', error);
    }
    
    return [];
  }

  async updateThreshold(historicalData) {
    if (!this.isTrained || historicalData.length < 20) {
      return;
    }

    const features = this.extractFeatures(historicalData);
    const errors = [];
    
    for (const feature of features) {
      const input =

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Auditoria de Segurança e Implementação

## 1. Auditoria de Código V9 e Plano de Ação

### Vulnerabilidades Identificadas na V9:
1. **Autenticação**: Sistema de sessão básico sem tokens JWT
2. **Input Validation**: Validação inconsistente de inputs
3. **Rate Limiting**: Ausente em endpoints críticos
4. **Dependências**: Múltiplas bibliotecas com CVEs conhecidos
5. **Logs**: Dados sensíveis em logs de erro
6. **CORS**: Configuração permissiva
7. **Headers de Segurança**: Ausentes

## 2. Estrutura do Projeto V10
