### src/server.js
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const xss = require('xss-clean');
const hpp = require('hpp');
const mongoSanitize = require('express-mongo-sanitize');
const dotenv = require('dotenv');

// Configuração de ambiente
dotenv.config();

// Importações de segurança
const securityHeaders = require('./security/headers');
const rateLimiter = require('./security/rate-limiter');
const inputSanitizer = require('./security/input-sanitizer');

// Importações de rotas
const authRoutes = require('./routes/auth-routes');
const apiRoutes = require('./routes/api-routes');

// Importação do logger
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Middleware de segurança
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"]
    }
  },
  hsts: {
    maxAge: 31536000,
    includeSubDomains: true,
    preload: true
  }
}));

app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['http://localhost:3000'],
  credentials: true,
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Requested-With']
}));

app.use(compression());
app.use(xss());
app.use(hpp());
app.use(mongoSanitize());

// Headers de segurança customizados
app.use(securityHeaders);

// Rate limiting global
app.use('/api/', rateLimiter.global);
app.use('/api/auth/', rateLimiter.auth);

// Parsers
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10kb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10kb' }));

// Sanitização de inputs
app.use(inputSanitizer);

// Rotas
app.use('/api/auth', authRoutes);
app.use('/api', apiRoutes);

// Rota de health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    version: '10.0.0'
  });
});

// Servir arquivos estáticos
app.use(express.static('public'));

// Middleware de erro
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  logger.error('Erro não tratado:', {
    error: err.message,
    stack: err.stack,
    path: req.path,
    method: req.method,
    ip: req.ip
  });

  // Não expor detalhes do erro em produção
  const errorResponse = {
    error: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'Internal Server Error' : err.message,
    status: 'error'
  };

  res.status(err.status || 500).json(errorResponse);
});

// 404 handler
app.use('*', (req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Endpoint não encontrado',
    path: req.originalUrl
  });
});

// Inicialização do servidor
if (require.main === module) {
  app.listen(PORT, () => {
    logger.info(`DIYAPP V10 rodando na porta ${PORT}`);
    logger.info(`Ambiente: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
    
    // Executar scan de segurança na inicialização
    if (process.env.RUN_SECURITY_SCAN_ON_START === 'true') {
      require('./security/sast-scanner').runScan();
    }
  });
}

module.exports = app;
```

### src/auth/oauth2.js
```javascript
const axios = require('axios');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class OAuth2Provider {
  constructor(config) {
    this.clientId = config.clientId;
    this.clientSecret = config.clientSecret;
    this.redirectUri = config.redirectUri;
    this.authorizationEndpoint = config.authorizationEndpoint;
    this.tokenEndpoint = config.tokenEndpoint;
    this.userInfoEndpoint = config.userInfoEndpoint;
    this.scopes = config.scopes || ['openid', 'profile', 'email'];
  }

  generateState() {
    return crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
  }

  generatePKCE() {
    const codeVerifier = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    const codeChallenge = crypto
      .createHash('sha256')
      .update(codeVerifier)
      .digest('base64')
      .replace(/\+/g, '-')
      .replace(/\//g, '_')
      .replace(/=/g, '');

    return { codeVerifier, codeChallenge };
  }

  getAuthorizationUrl(state, codeChallenge) {
    const params = new URLSearchParams({
      response_type: 'code',
      client_id: this.clientId,
      redirect_uri: this.redirectUri,
      scope: this.scopes.join(' '),
      state,
      code_challenge: codeChallenge,
      code_challenge_method: 'S256'
    });

    return `${this.authorizationEndpoint}?${params.toString()}`;
  }

  async exchangeCodeForToken(code, codeVerifier) {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(this.tokenEndpoint, {
        grant_type: 'authorization_code',
        code,
        redirect_uri: this.redirectUri,
        client_id: this.clientId,
        client_secret: this.clientSecret,
        code_verifier: codeVerifier
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na troca de código por token:', error.response?.data || error.message);
      throw new Error('Falha na autenticação OAuth2');
    }
  }

  async getUserInfo(accessToken) {
    try {
      const response = await axios.get(this.userInfoEndpoint, {
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro ao obter informações do usuário:', error.response?.data || error.message);
      throw new Error('Falha ao obter informações do usuário');
    }
  }

  validateIdToken(idToken) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.decode(idToken, { complete: true });
      
      // Validações básicas
      if (!decoded) {
        throw new Error('Token JWT inválido');
      }

      // Verificar issuer (iss)
      if (decoded.payload.iss !== this.issuer) {
        throw new Error('Issuer inválido');
      }

      // Verificar audience (aud)
      if (decoded.payload.aud !== this.clientId) {
        throw new Error('Audience inválido');
      }

      // Verificar expiração (exp)
      if (decoded.payload.exp < Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)) {
        throw new Error('Token expirado');
      }

      return decoded.payload;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na validação do ID Token:', error.message);
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

// Configuração para provedores comuns
const providers = {
  google: new OAuth2Provider({
    clientId: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID,
    clientSecret: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET,
    redirectUri: process.env.GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI,
    authorizationEndpoint: 'https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth',
    tokenEndpoint: 'https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token',
    userInfoEndpoint: 'https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/userinfo',
    issuer: 'https://accounts.google.com',
    scopes: ['openid', 'profile', 'email']
  }),

  github: new OAuth2Provider({
    clientId: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_ID,
    clientSecret: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET,
    redirectUri: process.env.GITHUB_REDIRECT_URI,
    authorizationEndpoint: 'https://github.com/login/oauth/authorize',
    tokenEndpoint: 'https://github.com/login/oauth/access_token',
    userInfoEndpoint: 'https://api.github.com/user',
    scopes: ['user:email', 'read:user']
  })
};

module.exports = { OAuth2Provider, providers };
```

### src/auth/jwt.js
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class JWTManager {
  constructor() {
    this.accessTokenSecret = process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    this.refreshTokenSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    this.accessTokenExpiry = process.env.JWT_ACCESS_EXPIRY || '15m';
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRY || '7d';
    
    // Blacklist de tokens revogados
    this.tokenBlacklist = new Set();
  }

  generateAccessToken(payload) {
    const tokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      type: 'access',
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
    };

    return jwt.sign(tokenPayload, this.accessTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: this.accessTokenExpiry,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });
  }

  generateRefreshToken(payload) {
    const tokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      type: 'refresh',
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
    };

    const token = jwt.sign(tokenPayload, this.refreshTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });

    // Gerar hash do refresh token para armazenamento seguro
    const tokenHash = crypto
      .createHash('sha256')
      .update(token)
      .digest('hex');

    return { token, hash: tokenHash };
  }

  verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      // Verificar se token está na blacklist
      if (this.tokenBlacklist.has(token)) {
        throw new Error('Token revogado');
      }

      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.accessTokenSecret, {
        algorithms: ['HS256']
      });

      if (decoded.type !== 'access') {
        throw new Error('Tipo de token inválido');
      }

      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na verificação do access token:', error.message);
      
      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        throw new Error('Token expirado');
      }
      
      if (error.name === 'JsonWebTokenError') {
        throw new Error('Token inválido');
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }

  verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.refreshTokenSecret, {
        algorithms: ['HS256']
      });

      if (decoded.type !== 'refresh') {
        throw new Error('Tipo de token inválido');
      }

      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na verificação do refresh token:', error.message);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  revokeToken(token) {
    try {
      // Decodificar sem verificar para obter expiração
      const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
      
      if (decoded && decoded.exp) {
        // Adicionar à blacklist até expirar
        this.tokenBlacklist.add(token);
        
        // Agendar remoção da blacklist após expiração
        const expiresIn = decoded.exp * 1000 - Date.now();
        if (expiresIn > 0) {
          setTimeout(() => {
            this.tokenBlacklist.delete(token);
          }, expiresIn);
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro ao revogar token:', error.message);
    }
  }

  rotateTokens(refreshToken) {
    try {
      const decoded = this.verifyRefreshToken(refreshToken);
      
      // Gerar novos tokens
      const newAccessToken = this.generateAccessToken({
        userId: decoded.userId,
        email: decoded.email,
        role: decoded.role
      });

      const newRefreshToken = this.generateRefreshToken({
        userId: decoded.userId,
        email: decoded.email,
        role: decoded.role
      });

      // Revogar o refresh token antigo
      this.revokeToken(refreshToken);

      return {
        accessToken: newAccessToken,
        refreshToken: newRefreshToken.token,
        refreshTokenHash: newRefreshToken.hash
      };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na rotação de tokens:', error.message);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Middleware de autenticação
  authenticate() {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      try {
        const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
        
        if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
          return res.status(401).json({
            error: 'Token de autenticação não fornecido',
            code: 'AUTH_TOKEN_MISSING'
          });
        }

        const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];
        const decoded = this.verifyAccessToken(token);

        // Adicionar informações do usuário à requisição
        req.user = {
          id: decoded.userId,
          email: decoded.email,
          role: decoded.role,
          permissions: decoded.permissions || []
        };

        // Ad

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]

## 1. Configuração do Módulo de Compliance

```javascript
module.exports = {
  // Configurações LGPD/GDPR
  dataRetention: {
    default: 730, // 2 anos em dias
    userData: 730,
    auditLogs: 1825, // 5 anos
    consentRecords: 1825 // 5 anos
  },
  
  // Bases legais conforme LGPD Art. 7
  legalBases: {
    CONSENT: 'consentimento',
    CONTRACT: 'contrato',
    LEGAL_OBLIGATION: 'obrigação_legal',
    VITAL_INTEREST: 'interesse_vital',
    PUBLIC_INTEREST: 'interesse_público',
    LEGITIMATE_INTEREST: 'legítimo_interesse'
  },
  
  // Categorias de dados pessoais
  dataCategories: {
    IDENTIFICATION: 'identificação',
    CONTACT: 'contato',
    FINANCIAL: 'financeiro',
    BEHAVIORAL: 'comportamental',
    TECHNICAL: 'técnico',
    SENSITIVE: 'sensível' // dados sensíveis conforme LGPD Art. 5º II
  },
  
  // Configurações de notificação
  notification: {
    dataBreach: {
      anpdDeadline: 72, // horas para notificar ANPD
      subjectDeadline: 15 // dias para comunicar titulares
    },
    dataSubjectRequests: {
      responseDeadline: 15, // dias para responder
      extensionDeadline: 15 // dias de prorrogação
    }
  },
  
  // Configurações de auditoria
  audit: {
    retentionDays: 1825,
    logLevels: ['INFO', 'WARN', 'ERROR', 'SECURITY', 'COMPLIANCE']
  }
};
```

## 2. Modelos de Dados de Compliance

```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const db = require('../../database/connection');
const config = require('../../../config/compliance-config');

const DataProcessingActivity = db.define('DataProcessingActivity', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  activityName: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(200),
    allowNull: false
  },
  description: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  purpose: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  dataCategories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  legalBasis: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(Object.values(config.legalBases)),
    allowNull: false
  },
  retentionPeriod: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: config.dataRetention.default
  },
  dataProcessors: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  internationalTransfer: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpiaRequired: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpiaConducted: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpiaDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE
  },
  riskLevel: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['baixo', 'médio', 'alto']),
    defaultValue: 'baixo'
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['ativo', 'inativo', 'revisão']),
    defaultValue: 'ativo'
  },
  createdAt: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  updatedAt: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'data_processing_activities',
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['activityName']
    },
    {
      fields: ['status']
    }
  ]
});

module.exports = DataProcessingActivity;
```

    }
  ]
});

  },

    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dataCategories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  severity: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical']),
    defaultValue: 'low'
  },
  details: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'audit_logs',
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['timestamp']
    },
    {
      fields: ['userId']
    },
    {
      fields: ['action']
    },
    {
      fields: ['complianceRelated']
    },
    {
      fields: ['level']
    }
  ]
});

module.exports = AuditLog;

## 3. Serviços de Compliance

**src/compliance/services/DataMappingService.js**
```javascript
const DataProcessingActivity = require('../models/DataProcessingActivity');
const AuditLog = require('../models/AuditLog');
const config = require('../../../config/compliance-config');

class DataMappingService {
  constructor() {
    this.dataFlows = new Map();
  }

  /**
   * Registra um novo fluxo de dados no ROPA (Registro de Atividades de Processamento)
   */
  async registerDataFlow(flowData) {
    try {
      // Validação dos dados obrigatórios
      this.validateFlowData(flowData);

      // Verifica se já existe atividade similar
      const existingActivity = await DataProcessingActivity.findOne({
        where: {
          activityName: flowData.activityName,
          status: 'ativo'
        }
      });

      if (existingActivity) {
        throw new Error('Já existe uma atividade de processamento com este nome');
      }

      // Determina se DPIA é necessária
      const requiresDPIA = this.requiresDPIA(flowData);

      // Cria o registro no ROPA
      const activity = await DataProcessingActivity.create({
        ...flowData,
        dpiaRequired: requiresDPIA,
        riskLevel: this.calculateRiskLevel(flowData)
      });

      // Log de auditoria
      await AuditLog.create({
        level: 'COMPLIANCE',
        action: 'DATA_FLOW_REGISTERED',
        resourceType: 'DataProcessingActivity',
        resourceId: activity.id,
        complianceRelated: true,
        dataCategories: flowData.dataCategories,
        details: `Novo fluxo de dados registrado: ${flowData.activityName}`,
        changes: flowData
      });

      // Mapeia internamente para cache
      this.dataFlows.set(activity.id, {
        ...activity.toJSON(),
        processors: flowData.dataProcessors || []
      });

      return activity;
    } catch (error) {
      await AuditLog.create({
        level: 'ERROR',
        action: 'DATA_FLOW_REGISTRATION_FAILED',
        complianceRelated: true,
        details: `Falha ao registrar fluxo de dados: ${error.message}`,
        severity: 'high'
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Valida dados do fluxo conforme LGPD
   */
  validateFlowData(flowData) {
    const requiredFields = [
      'activityName',
      'description',
      'purpose',
      'dataCategories',
      'legalBasis'
    ];

    for (const field of requiredFields) {
      if (!flowData[field]) {
        throw new Error(`Campo obrigatório não informado: ${field}`);
      }
    }

    // Valida base legal
    if (!Object.values(config.legalBases).includes(flowData.legalBasis)) {
      throw new Error('Base legal inválida');
    }

    // Valida categorias de dados
    if (!Array.isArray(flowData.dataCategories)) {
      throw new Error('dataCategories deve ser um array');
    }

    // Valida dados sensíveis
    if (flowData.dataCategories.includes(config.dataCategories.SENSITIVE)) {
      if (flowData.legalBasis !== config.legalBases.CONSENT) {
        throw new Error('Dados sensíveis exigem base legal de consentimento');
      }
    }

    return true;
  }

  /**
   * Determina se DPIA é necessária conforme GDPR Art. 35
   */
  requiresDPIA(flowData) {
    const highRiskIndicators = [
      // Processamento sistemático e extensivo
      flowData.dataCategories?.length > 5,
      
      // Dados sensíveis
      flowData.dataCategories?.includes(config.dataCategories.SENSITIVE),
      
      // Monitoramento sistemático de área publicamente acessível
      flowData.purpose?.toLowerCase().includes('monitoramento'),
      flowData.purpose?.toLowerCase().includes('vigilância'),
      
      // Decisões automatizadas com efeito legal
      flowData.description?.toLowerCase().includes('decisão automatizada'),
      flowData.description?.toLowerCase().includes('perfilamento'),
      
      // Transferência internacional para países sem adequação
      flowData.internationalTransfer === true &&
      !this.isAdequateCountry(flowData.destinationCountry),
      
      // Processamento em larga escala
      flowData.estimatedVolume > 100000
    ];

    return highRiskIndicators.some(indicator => indicator === true);
  }

  /**
   * Calcula nível de risco do processamento
   */
  calculateRiskLevel(flowData) {
    let riskScore = 0;

    // Dados sensíveis: +3 pontos
    if (flowData.dataCategories?.includes(config.dataCategories.SENSITIVE)) {
      riskScore += 3;
    }

    // Transferência internacional: +2 pontos
    if (flowData.internationalTransfer) {
      riskScore += 2;
    }

    // Múltiplos processadores: +1 ponto
    if (flowData.dataProcessors?.length > 2) {
      riskScore += 1;
    }

    // Retenção longa: +1 ponto
    if (flowData.retentionPeriod > 365 * 5) { // Mais de 5 anos
      riskScore += 1;
    }

    // Determina nível baseado no score
    if (riskScore >= 3) return 'alto';
    if (riskScore >= 1) return 'médio';
    return 'baixo';
  }

  /**
   * Gera relatório de mapeamento de dados
   */
  async generateDataMappingReport() {
    const activities = await DataProcessingActivity.findAll({
      where: { status: 'ativo' },
      order: [['riskLevel

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura como Código

### `terraform/main.tf`

```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key    = "v10/terraform.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

# VPC Module
module "vpc" {
  source = "./modules/vpc"
  
  environment = var.environment
  vpc_cidr    = var.vpc_cidr
  azs         = var.availability_zones
  
  public_subnet_cidrs  = var.public_subnet_cidrs
  private_subnet_cidrs = var.private_subnet_cidrs
}

# EKS Cluster Module
module "eks" {
  source = "./modules/eks"
  
  environment          = var.environment
  cluster_name         = "diyapp-${var.environment}"
  vpc_id              = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnet_ids  = module.vpc.private_subnet_ids
  public_subnet_ids   = module.vpc.public_subnet_ids
  
  node_instance_types = var.node_instance_types
  min_node_count     = var.min_node_count
  max_node_count     = var.max_node_count
  desired_node_count = var.desired_node_count
}

# RDS PostgreSQL Module
module "rds" {
  source = "./modules/rds"
  
  environment      = var.environment
  vpc_id          = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids      = module.vpc.private_subnet_ids
  security_groups = [module.eks.cluster_security_group_id]
  
  instance_class    = var.rds_instance_class
  allocated_storage = var.rds_allocated_storage
  database_name     = var.rds_database_name
  username          = var.rds_username
}

# Monitoring Module
module "monitoring" {
  source = "./modules/monitoring"
  
  environment  = var.environment
  cluster_name = module.eks.cluster_name
  vpc_id       = module.vpc.vpc_id
}

# Outputs
output "cluster_endpoint" {
  value = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
}

output "cluster_certificate_authority_data" {
  value = module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data
}

output "rds_endpoint" {
  value = module.rds.endpoint
}

output "grafana_endpoint" {
  value = module.monitoring.grafana_endpoint
}

output "prometheus_endpoint" {
  value = module.monitoring.prometheus_endpoint
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`

```hcl
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (dev, staging, prod)"
  type        = string
  default     = "dev"
}

variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
}

variable "public_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "Public subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
}

variable "private_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "Private subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.4.0/24", "10.0.5.0/24", "10.0.6.0/24"]
}

variable "node_instance_types" {
  description = "EKS node instance types"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["t3.medium", "t3.large"]
}

variable "min_node_count" {
  description = "Minimum number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 2
}

variable "max_node_count" {
  description = "Maximum number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 10
}

variable "desired_node_count" {
  description = "Desired number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 3
}

variable "rds_instance_class" {
  description = "RDS instance class"
  type        = string
  default     = "db.t3.medium"
}

variable "rds_allocated_storage" {
  description = "RDS allocated storage in GB"
  type        = number
  default     = 20
}

variable "rds_database_name" {
  description = "RDS database name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp"
}

variable "rds_username" {
  description = "RDS username"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_admin"
}
```

### `terraform/modules/eks/main.tf`

```hcl
resource "aws_eks_cluster" "cluster" {
  name     = var.cluster_name
  role_arn = aws_iam_role.cluster.arn
  version  = "1.28"

  vpc_config {
    subnet_ids              = concat(var.public_subnet_ids, var.private_subnet_ids)
    endpoint_private_access = true
    endpoint_public_access  = true
    public_access_cidrs     = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  enabled_cluster_log_types = [
    "api",
    "audit",
    "authenticator",
    "controllerManager",
    "scheduler"
  ]

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Name        = var.cluster_name
  }
}

resource "aws_eks_node_group" "nodes" {
  cluster_name    = aws_eks_cluster.cluster.name
  node_group_name = "${var.cluster_name}-node-group"
  node_role_arn   = aws_iam_role.nodes.arn
  subnet_ids      = var.private_subnet_ids

  scaling_config {
    desired_size = var.desired_node_count
    max_size     = var.max_node_count
    min_size     = var.min_node_count
  }

  instance_types = var.node_instance_types

  update_config {
    max_unavailable = 1
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

# IAM Roles and Policies
resource "aws_iam_role" "cluster" {
  name = "${var.cluster_name}-cluster-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Statement = [{
      Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
      Effect = "Allow"
      Principal = {
        Service = "eks.amazonaws.com"
      }
    }]
    Version = "2012-10-17"
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "nodes" {
  name = "${var.cluster_name}-node-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Statement = [{
      Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
      Effect = "Allow"
      Principal = {
        Service = "ec2.amazonaws.com"
      }
    }]
    Version = "2012-10-17"
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "cluster_policy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSClusterPolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.cluster.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "node_policy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.nodes.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "cni_policy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.nodes.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "ecr_policy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly"
  role       = aws_iam_role.nodes.name
}

output "cluster_name" {
  value = aws_eks_cluster.cluster.name
}

output "cluster_endpoint" {
  value = aws_eks_cluster.cluster.endpoint
}

output "cluster_certificate_authority_data" {
  value = aws_eks_cluster.cluster.certificate_authority[0].data
}

output "cluster_security_group_id" {
  value = aws_eks_cluster.cluster.vpc_config[0].cluster_security_group_id
}
```

### `kubernetes/deployments/diyapp-api.yaml`

```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v10
    squad: autonomous-sre
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v10
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "3000"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: diyapp-api
        image: diyapp/api:v10.0.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        - containerPort: 3001
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: database-url
        - name: REDIS_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: redis-url
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /startup
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 0
          periodSeconds: 10
          failureThreshold: 30
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config-volume
          mountPath: /app/config
      volumes:
      - name: config-volume
        configMap:
          name: diyapp-config
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 100
            podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - diyapp-api
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
---
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-hpa
  namespace: diyapp
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: diyapp-api
  minReplicas: 3
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
  - type: Pods
    pods:
      metric:
        name: http_requests_per_second
      target:
        type: AverageValue
        averageValue: 100
```

### `kubernetes/services/diyapp-api-service.yaml`

```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  annotations:
    prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
    prometheus.io/port: "3001"
    external-dns.alpha.kubernetes.io/hostname: api.diyapp.com
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - name: http
    port: 80
    targetPort: 3000
    protocol: TCP
  - name: metrics
    port: 3001
    targetPort: 3001
    protocol: TCP
  type: LoadBalancer
---
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-ingress
  namespace: diyapp
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: nginx
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: letsencrypt-prod
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "50m"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-read-timeout: "300"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-send-timeout: "300"
spec:
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - api.diyapp.com
    secretName: diyapp-tls
  rules:
  - host: api.diyapp.com
    http:
      paths:
      - path: /
        pathType: Prefix
        backend:
          service:
            name: diyapp-api
            port:
              number: 80
```

## 3. Docker Configuration

### `docker/diyapp/Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Install dependencies
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Build application
RUN npm run build

# Production stage
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Install runtime dependencies
RUN apk add --no-cache tini curl

# Copy built application
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/package.json ./package.json

# Create non-root user
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001 && \
    chown -R nodejs:nodejs /app

USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=40s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Expose ports
EXPOSE 3000 3001

# Use tini as init process
ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]

# Start application
CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]
```



### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Data Engineering Pipeline Optimization

## Visão Geral
Refatoração completa dos pipelines de dados da V9 para garantir qualidade, latência mínima e escalabilidade. Implementação de data warehouse otimizado para analytics de performance com foco em estabilidade 100% autônoma.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-data-pipeline/
├── dbt/
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── staging/
│   │   │   ├── schema.yml

## 1. Configuração do Data Warehouse (PostgreSQL + TimescaleDB)

### docker-compose.yml
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: timescale/timescaledb:latest-pg14
    container_name: diyapp_data_warehouse
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_warehouse
      POSTGRES_USER: data_engineer
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    networks:
      - data_network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U data_engineer -d diyapp_warehouse"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  airflow:
    image: apache/airflow:2.7.0
    container_name: diyapp_airflow
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__DATABASE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres:5432/airflow_db
      AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
      AIRFLOW__WEBSERVER__SECRET_KEY: ${AIRFLOW_SECRET_KEY}
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/config:/opt/airflow/config
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    networks:
      - data_network
    command: >
      bash -c "
        airflow db init &&
        airflow users create --username admin --password admin --firstname Admin --lastname User --role Admin --email admin@diyapp.com &&
        airflow scheduler &
        airflow webserver
      "

  metabase:
    image: metabase/metabase:latest
    container_name: diyapp_metabase
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      MB_DB_TYPE: postgres
      MB_DB_DBNAME: metabase
      MB_DB_PORT: 5432
      MB_DB_HOST: postgres
      MB_DB_USER: metabase_user
      MB_DB_PASS: ${METABASE_PASSWORD}
    depends_on:
      - postgres
    networks:
      - data_network

networks:
  data_network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

### scripts/init.sql
```sql
-- Inicialização do Data Warehouse
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts;

-- Usuários e permissões
CREATE USER metabase_user WITH PASSWORD '${METABASE_PASSWORD}';
CREATE USER airflow_user WITH PASSWORD '${AIRFLOW_PASSWORD}';
CREATE USER dbt_user WITH PASSWORD '${DBT_PASSWORD}';

-- Permissões
GRANT CONNECT ON DATABASE diyapp_warehouse TO metabase_user, airflow_user, dbt_user;
GRANT USAGE ON SCHEMA raw, staging, marts TO metabase_user, airflow_user, dbt_user;
GRANT SELECT ON ALL TABLES IN SCHEMA raw, staging, marts TO metabase_user;
GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON ALL TABLES IN SCHEMA raw, staging, marts TO dbt_user;

-- Tabelas raw (bronze layer)
CREATE TABLE raw.events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    event_type VARCHAR(100),
    event_data JSONB,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ,
    source_system VARCHAR(100),
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE raw.llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id VARCHAR(255),
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    provider VARCHAR(50),
    prompt_tokens INTEGER,
    completion_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status_code INTEGER,
    request_body JSONB,
    response_body JSONB,
    called_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE raw.users (
    user_id VARCHAR(255) PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    last_seen_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    metadata JSONB,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE raw.api_logs (
    log_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    endpoint VARCHAR(255),
    method VARCHAR(10),
    status_code INTEGER,
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    user_agent TEXT,
    ip_address INET,
    logged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Índices para performance
CREATE INDEX idx_events_timestamp ON raw.events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_user ON raw.events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_called_at ON raw.llm_calls(called_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_model ON raw.llm_calls(model_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_api_logs_logged_at ON raw.api_logs(logged_at);

-- Tabela de auditoria de pipeline
CREATE TABLE monitoring.pipeline_runs (
    run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(100),
    status VARCHAR(20),
    records_processed INTEGER,
    started_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    error_message TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Tabela de alertas de qualidade
CREATE TABLE monitoring.data_quality_alerts (
    alert_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    dataset_name VARCHAR(100),
    test_name VARCHAR(100),
    severity VARCHAR(20),
    description TEXT,
    records_affected INTEGER,
    alert_triggered_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    acknowledged BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);
```

## 2. Configuração dbt (Data Build Tool)

### dbt/dbt_project.yml
```yaml
name: diyapp_v10
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: diyapp_v10

model-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
seed-paths: ["data"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v10:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      schema: staging
      tags: ["staging"]
    marts:
      materialized: table
      schema: marts
      tags: ["marts"]
      product:
        materialized: table
        schema: marts
        tags: ["marts", "product"]
      ai:
        materialized: table
        schema: marts
        tags: ["marts", "ai"]
      ops:
        materialized: table
        schema: marts
        tags: ["marts", "ops"]

seeds:
  diyapp_v10:
    schema: raw
    materialized: table

tests:
  diyapp_v10:
    data_quality:
      severity: warn
    custom:
      severity: error

vars:
  start_date: "2024-01-01"
  timezone: "UTC"
  currency: "USD"
```

### dbt/models/staging/schema.yml
```yaml
version: 2

sources:
  - name: raw
    schema: raw
    tables:
      - name: events
        description: "Raw events from application"
        loaded_at_field: ingested_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
      - name: llm_calls
        description: "Raw LLM API calls from gateway"
        loaded_at_field: ingested_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 30, period: minute}
          error_after: {count: 60, period: minute}
      - name: users
        description: "Raw user data"
        loaded_at_field: ingested_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 24, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 48, period: hour}
      - name: api_logs
        description: "Raw API access logs"
        loaded_at_field: ingested_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 15, period: minute}
          error_after: {count: 30, period: minute}

models:
  - name: stg_events
    description: "Cleaned and standardized events data"
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        description: "Unique event identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: user_id
        description: "User identifier"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: event_type
        description: "Type of event"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['page_view', 'button_click', 'form_submit', 'api_call', 'error']
      - name: event_timestamp
        description: "Timestamp when event occurred"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: ingested_at
        description: "Timestamp when data was ingested"
  
  - name: stg_llm_calls
    description: "Cleaned and standardized LLM calls data"
    columns:
      - name: call_id
        description: "Unique call identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: model_name
        description: "LLM model used"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: total_tokens
        description: "Total tokens consumed"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - relationships:
              to: ref('stg_events')
              field: event_id
      - name: cost_usd
        description: "Cost in USD"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - dbt_utils.expression_is_true:
              expression: "cost_usd >= 0"
      - name: latency_ms
        description: "Response latency in milliseconds"
        tests:
          - dbt_utils.expression_is_true:
              expression: "latency_ms > 0 and latency_ms < 30000"
```

### dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging']
    )
}}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        event_data,
        event_timestamp,
        source_system,
        ingested_at
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= '{{ var("start_date") }}'
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        -- Standardize event_id
        CAST(event_id AS UUID) AS event_id,
        
        -- Clean user_id
        CASE 
            WHEN user_id IS NULL THEN 'anonymous'
            WHEN user_id = '' THEN 'anonymous'
            ELSE TRIM(user_id)
        END AS user_id,
        
        -- Standardize event_type
        LOWER(TRIM(event_type)) AS event_type,
        
        -- Parse event_data JSON
        event_data,
        
        -- Ensure timestamp is timezone aware
        CASE
            WHEN event_timestamp IS NULL THEN ingested_at
            ELSE event_timestamp AT TIME ZONE '{{ var("timezone") }}'
        END AS event_timestamp,
        
        -- Source system
        COALESCE(source_system, 'unknown') AS source_system,
        
        -- Metadata
        ingested_at,
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date
        
    FROM source
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned
```

### dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='marts',
        tags=['marts', 'product']
    )
}}

WITH daily_users AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT event_id) AS event_count,
        ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT event_type) AS event_types
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

daily_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN 'page_view' = ANY(event_types) THEN user_id END) AS page_view_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN 'button_click' = ANY(event_types) THEN user_id END) AS interaction_users,
        AVG(event_count) AS avg_events_per_user,
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY event_count) AS median_events_per_user
    FROM daily_users
    GROUP BY 1
),

rolling_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        active_users,
        page_view_users,
        interaction_users,
        avg_events_per_user,
        median_events_per_user,
        AVG(active_users) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS weekly_avg_active_users,
        AVG(active_users) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 29 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS monthly_avg_active_users
    FROM daily_metrics
)

SELECT
    date,
    active_users,
    page_view_users,
    interaction_users,
    avg_events_per_user,
    median_events_per_user,
    weekly_avg_active_users,
    monthly_avg_active_users,
    ROUND(100.0 * page_view_users / NULLIF(active_users, 0), 2) AS page_view_rate,
    ROUND(100.0 * interaction_users / NULLIF(active_users

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Auto-Scaling e Anomaly Detection

Vou implementar um sistema completo de auto-scaling baseado em carga, detecção de anomalias para métricas de sistema e automação de rollback. O sistema será projetado para operação 100% autônoma.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── index.html
├── package.json
├── src/
│   ├── auto-scaling/
│   │   ├── scaling-controller.js
│   │   ├── load-monitor.js
│   │   └── scaling-strategies.js
│   ├── anomaly-detection/
│   │   ├── anomaly-detector.js
│   │   ├── metrics-collector.js
│   │   └── anomaly-rules.js
│   ├── auto-rollback/
│   │   ├── rollback-controller.js
│   │   ├── health-checker.js
│   │   └── version-manager.js
│   ├── dashboard/
│   │   ├── dashboard-server.js
│   │   └── dashboard-ui.js
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── config-manager.js
│   └── utils/
│       ├── logger.js
│       └── alert-manager.js
├── public/
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── dashboard.css
│   └── js/
│       └── dashboard.js
├── tests/
│   ├── scaling-tests.js
│   └── anomaly-tests.js
└── README.md
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Auditoria de Segurança e Implementações

## 1. Análise de Segurança da V9

### Vulnerabilidades Identificadas na V9:
1. **Autenticação**: Sistema baseado em sessão sem tokens JWT, sem expiração adequada
2. **Input Validation**: Validação básica sem sanitização profunda
3. **Rate Limiting**: Ausente em endpoints críticos
4. **Dependências**: Múltiplas bibliotecas com CVEs conhecidos
5. **CORS**: Configuração permissiva
6. **Logs**: Informações sensíveis em logs de erro

## 2. Estrutura do Projeto V10

```
diyapp-v10/
├── src/
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── oauth2.js
│   │   ├── jwt.js
│   │   └── middleware.js
│   ├── security/
│   │   ├── input-sanitizer.js
│   │   ├── rate-limiter.js
│   │   └── vulnerability-scanner.js
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── auth-controller.js
│   │   └── api-controller.js
│   ├── models/
│   │   └── user.js
│   └── config/
│       └── security.js
├── public/
│   ├── index.html
│   └── dashboard.html
├── tests/
│   └── security.test.js
├── package.json
├── docker-compose.yml
└── README.md
```

## 3. Implementação Completa

### 3.1 package.json (Atualizado com dependências seguras)

```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v10",
  "version": "10.0.0",
  "description": "DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core with enhanced security",
  "main": "src/server.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/server.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/server.js",
    "test": "jest",
    "security-scan": "npm audit && npx snyk test",
    "lint": "eslint src/",
    "docker-build": "docker build -t diyapp-v10 .",
    "docker-up": "docker-compose up -d"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "express": "^4.18.2",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.2",
    "bcrypt": "^5.1.1",
    "helmet": "^7.1.0",
    "express-rate-limit": "^7.1.5",
    "express-validator": "^7.0.1",
    "cors": "^2.8.5",
    "sqlite3": "^5.1.6",
    "winston": "^3.11.0",
    "uuid": "^9.0.1",
    "axios": "^1.6.2",
    "dotenv": "^16.3.1",
    "express-session": "^1.17.3",

### 3.2 src/config/security.js

```javascript
// Configurações de segurança centralizadas
const securityConfig = {
  // JWT Configuration
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key-change-in-production',
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m',
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',
    issuer: 'diyapp-v10',
    audience: 'diyapp-users'
  },
  
  // OAuth2 Configuration
  oauth2: {
    google: {
      clientId: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET,
      callbackURL: process.env.GOOGLE_CALLBACK_URL || 'http://localhost:3000/auth/google/callback'
    },
    github: {
      clientId: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET,
      callbackURL: process.env.GITHUB_CALLBACK_URL || 'http://localhost:3000/auth/github/callback'
    }
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting Configuration
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
    standardHeaders: true,
    legacyHeaders: false,
    skipSuccessfulRequests: false
  },
  
  // CORS Configuration
  cors: {
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['http://localhost:3000'],
    methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
    allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Requested-With'],
    credentials: true,
    maxAge: 86400 // 24 hours
  },
  
  // Input Validation Rules
  validation: {
    username: {
      min: 3,
      max: 30,
      regex: /^[a-zA-Z0-9_]+$/
    },
    password: {
      min: 12,
      requireUppercase: true,
      requireLowercase: true,
      requireNumbers: true,
      requireSpecialChars: true
    },
    email: {
      regex: /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/
    }
  },
  
  // Security Headers
  headers: {
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://fonts.googleapis.com"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'", "https://fonts.gstatic.com"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"]
    },
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000, // 1 year
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    }
  }
};

module.exports = securityConfig;
```

### 3.3 src/auth/jwt.js

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

class JWTManager {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = securityConfig.jwt.secret;
    this.issuer = securityConfig.jwt.issuer;
    this.audience = securityConfig.jwt.audience;
  }

  // Generate access token
  generateAccessToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      role: user.role,
      permissions: user.permissions,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex') // Unique token ID for revocation
    };

    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenExpiry,
      issuer: this.issuer,
      audience: this.audience
    });
  }

  // Generate refresh token
  generateRefreshToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      type: 'refresh'
    };

    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenExpiry,
      issuer: this.issuer,
      audience: this.audience
    });
  }

  // Verify token
  verifyToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
        issuer: this.issuer,
        audience: this.audience
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Token verification failed: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Decode token without verification (for inspection)
  decodeToken(token) {
    return jwt.decode(token);
  }

  // Check if token is expired
  isTokenExpired(token) {
    try {
      this.verifyToken(token);
      return false;
    } catch (error) {
      return error.name === 'TokenExpiredError';
    }
  }

  // Generate token pair
  generateTokenPair(user) {
    return {
      accessToken: this.generateAccessToken(user),
      refreshToken: this.generateRefreshToken(user),
      tokenType: 'Bearer',
      expiresIn: 900 // 15 minutes in seconds
    };
  }

  // Rotate refresh token
  rotateRefreshToken(oldRefreshToken, user) {
    try {
      const decoded = this.verifyToken(oldRefreshToken);
      
      if (decoded.type !== 'refresh') {
        throw new Error('Invalid token type');
      }

      // Blacklist old token (in production, store in Redis)
      this.blacklistToken(oldRefreshToken);

      return this.generateRefreshToken(user);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Refresh token rotation failed: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Blacklist token (simplified - in production use Redis)
  blacklistToken(token) {
    // In production, store in Redis with TTL
    const decoded = this.decodeToken(token);
    if (decoded && decoded.exp) {
      const ttl = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      if (ttl > 0) {
        // Store token ID in blacklist
        console.log(`Token ${decoded.jti} blacklisted for ${ttl} seconds`);
      }
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTManager();
```

### 3.4 src/auth/oauth2.js

```javascript
const axios = require('axios');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

class OAuth2Manager {
  constructor() {
    this.providers = {
      google: this.setupGoogle(),
      github: this.setupGithub()
    };
  }

  setupGoogle() {
    return {
      authUrl: 'https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth',
      tokenUrl: 'https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token',
      userInfoUrl: 'https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/userinfo',
      clientId: securityConfig.oauth2.google.clientId,
      clientSecret: securityConfig.oauth2.google.clientSecret,
      callbackURL: securityConfig.oauth2.google.callbackURL,
      scope: ['openid', 'email', 'profile']
    };
  }

  setupGithub() {
    return {
      authUrl: 'https://github.com/login/oauth/authorize',
      tokenUrl: 'https://github.com/login/oauth/access_token',
      userInfoUrl: 'https://api.github.com/user',
      clientId: securityConfig.oauth2.github.clientId,
      clientSecret: securityConfig.oauth2.github.clientSecret,
      callbackURL: securityConfig.oauth2.github.callbackURL,
      scope: ['user:email']
    };
  }

  // Generate state parameter for CSRF protection
  generateState() {
    return crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
  }

  // Generate PKCE code verifier and challenge
  generatePKCE() {
    const codeVerifier = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('base64url');
    const codeChallenge = crypto
      .createHash('sha256')
      .update(codeVerifier)
      .digest('base64url');
    
    return { codeVerifier, codeChallenge };
  }

  // Get authorization URL
  getAuthorizationUrl(providerName, state, codeChallenge = null) {
    const provider = this.providers[providerName];
    if (!provider) {
      throw new Error(`Unsupported OAuth2 provider: ${providerName}`);
    }

    const params = new URLSearchParams({
      client_id: provider.clientId,
      redirect_uri: provider.callbackURL,
      response_type: 'code',
      scope: provider.scope.join(' '),
      state: state,
      ...(codeChallenge && {
        code_challenge: codeChallenge,
        code_challenge_method: 'S256'
      })
    });

    return `${provider.authUrl}?${params.toString()}`;
  }

  // Exchange authorization code for tokens
  async exchangeCode(providerName, code, codeVerifier = null) {
    const provider = this.providers[providerName];
    
    const data = {
      client_id: provider.clientId,
      client_secret: provider.clientSecret,
      code: code,
      redirect_uri: provider.callbackURL,
      grant_type: 'authorization_code',
      ...(codeVerifier && { code_verifier: codeVerifier })
    };

    try {
      const response = await axios.post(provider.tokenUrl, data, {
        headers: {
          'Accept': 'application/json',
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('OAuth2 token exchange failed:', error.response?.data || error.message);
      throw new Error('Failed to exchange authorization code');
    }
  }

  // Get user info from provider
  async getUserInfo(providerName, accessToken) {
    const provider = this.providers[providerName];
    
    try {
      const response = await axios.get(provider.userInfoUrl, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${accessToken}`,
          'Accept': 'application/json'
        }
      });

      return this.normalizeUserInfo(providerName, response.data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch user info:', error.response?.data || error.message);
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch user information');
    }
  }

  // Normalize user info from different providers
  normalizeUserInfo(providerName, userInfo) {
    const baseInfo = {
      provider: providerName,
      providerId: userInfo.id || userInfo.sub,
      email: userInfo.email,
      emailVerified: userInfo.email_verified || userInfo.verified || false
    };

    switch (providerName) {
      case 'google':
        return {
          ...baseInfo,
          name: userInfo.name,
          givenName: userInfo.given_name,
          familyName: userInfo.family_name,
          picture: userInfo.picture,
          locale: userInfo.locale
        };
      
      case 'github':
        return {
          ...baseInfo,
          name: userInfo.name,
          login: userInfo.login,
          avatarUrl: userInfo.avatar_url,
          bio: userInfo.bio,
          location: userInfo.location
        };
      
      default:
        return baseInfo;
    }
  }

  // Validate state parameter (CSRF protection)
  validateState(receivedState, originalState) {
    if (!receivedState || !originalState) {
      return false;
    }
    return crypto.timingSafeEqual(
      Buffer.from(receivedState),
      Buffer.from(originalState)
    );
  }
}

module.exports = new OAuth2Manager();
```

### 3.5 src/security/input-sanitizer.js

```javascript
const { body, validationResult, sanitizeBody } = require('express-validator');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');
const xss = require('xss');

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    this.xssOptions = {
      whiteList: {}, // empty, means filter out all tags
      stripIgnoreTag: true, // filter out all HTML not in the whitelist
      stripIgnoreTagBody: ['script', 'style'] // the script and style tag and its content
    };
  }

  // Common validation rules
  get commonRules() {
    return [
      // Trim all fields
      body('*').trim(),
      
      // Escape HTML entities
      body('*').escape(),
      
      // Validate content type
      body('*').isString().withMessage('Invalid input type'),
      
      // Check for null bytes (common in injection attacks)
      body('*').custom(value => {
        if (value && value.includes('\0')) {
          throw new Error('Null bytes are not allowed');
        }
        return true;
      })
    ];
  }

  // User registration validation
  get userRegistrationRules() {
    return [
      ...this.commonRules,
      
      body('username')
        .isLength({ min: securityConfig.validation.username.min, max: securityConfig.validation.username.max })
        .withMessage(`Username must be between ${securityConfig.validation.username.min} and ${securityConfig.validation.username.max} characters`)
        .matches(securityConfig.validation.username.regex)
        .withMessage('Username can only contain letters, numbers, and underscores'),
      
      body('email')
        .isEmail()
        .withMessage('Invalid email address')
        .normalizeEmail(),
      
      body('password')
        .isLength({ min: securityConfig.validation.password.min })
        .withMessage(`Password must be at least ${securityConfig.validation.password.min} characters`)
        .matches(/[A-Z]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one uppercase letter')
        .matches(/[a-z]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one lowercase letter')
        .matches(/[0-9]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one number')
        .matches(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one special character'),
      
      body('confirmPassword')
        .custom((value, { req }) => value === req.body.password)
        .withMessage('Passwords do not match')
    ];
  }

  // Login validation
  get loginRules() {
    return [
      ...this.commonRules,
      
      body('email')
        .isEmail()
        .withMessage('Invalid email address')
        .normalizeEmail(),
      
      body('password')
        .notEmpty()
        .withMessage('Password is required')
    ];
  }

  // API input validation
  get apiInputRules() {
    return [
      ...this.commonRules,
      
      body('*.id').optional().isInt({ min: 1 }).withMessage('ID must be a positive integer'),
      body('*.limit').optional().isInt({ min: 1, max: 100 }).

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Módulo de Compliance LGPD/GDPR

Vou implementar um sistema completo de compliance para a V10, focando em mapeamento de fluxo de dados, gerenciamento de consentimento e logs de auditoria. O sistema será totalmente funcional e pronto para produção.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-compliance/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard de Compliance
├── package.json
├── .env.example
├── src/
│   ├── server.js                 # Servidor principal
│   ├── config/
│   │   ├── database.js           # Configuração do banco
│   │   └── compliance.js         # Configurações de compliance
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── DataFlow.js           # Mapeamento de fluxo de dados
│   │   ├── Consent.js            # Gerenciamento de consentimento
│   │   ├── AuditLog.js           # Logs de auditoria
│   │   └── DataSubject.js        # Titulares de dados
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── complianceController.js
│   │   ├── consentController.js
│   │   └── auditController.js
│   ├── routes/
│   │   ├── complianceRoutes.js
│   │   └── apiRoutes.js
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── auditMiddleware.js    # Middleware de logs automáticos
│   │   └── complianceMiddleware.js
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── dataMappingService.js
│   │   ├── consentService.js
│   │   └── notificationService.js
│   ├── utils/
│   │   ├── validators.js
│   │   └── encryption.js
│   └── public/
│       ├── css/
│       │   └── style.css
│       └── js/
│           └── dashboard.js
└── scripts/
    ├── init-db.js                # Script de inicialização
    └── generate-dpia.js          # Gerador de DPIA
```

## 3. src/server.js

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const session = require('express-session');
const path = require('path');
require('dotenv').config();

// Configurações
const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Middleware de segurança
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
    },
  },
}));

app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Sessão
app.use(session({
  secret: process.env.SESSION_SECRET || 'compliance-secret-key',
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: false,
  cookie: { 
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
    httpOnly: true,
    maxAge: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 24 horas
  }
}));

// Middleware de auditoria automática
const auditMiddleware = require('./middleware/auditMiddleware');
app.use(auditMiddleware);

// Middleware de compliance
const complianceMiddleware = require('./middleware/complianceMiddleware');
app.use(complianceMiddleware);

// Banco de dados
const db = require('./config/database');
db.authenticate()
  .then(() => {
    console.log('✅ Banco de dados conectado');
    return db.sync({ alter: true });
  })
  .then(() => console.log('✅ Modelos sincronizados'))
  .catch(err => console.error('❌ Erro no banco:', err));

// Rotas
const complianceRoutes = require('./routes/complianceRoutes');
const apiRoutes = require('./routes/apiRoutes');

app.use('/api/compliance', complianceRoutes);
app.use('/api', apiRoutes);

// Arquivos estáticos
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Dashboard principal
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ 
    status: 'healthy',
    compliance: 'active',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  });
});

// Inicialização
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`🚀 Servidor de Compliance rodando na porta ${PORT}`);
  console.log(`📊 Dashboard: http://localhost:${PORT}`);
  console.log(`🔒 Modo: ${process.env.NODE_ENV}`);
});
```

    acquire: 30000,
    idle: 10000
  }

## 6. src/models/DataFlow.js

```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');
const { DATA_CATEGORIES } = require('../config/compliance');

const DataFlow = sequelize.define('DataFlow', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  flow_name: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  description: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  data_categories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: [],
    validate: {
      isValidCategories(value) {
        if (!Array.isArray(value)) {
          throw new Error('Data categories must be an array');
        }
        value.forEach(cat => {
          if (!Object.values(DATA_CATEGORIES).includes(cat)) {
            throw new Error(`Invalid data category: ${cat}`);
          }
        });
      }
    }
  },
  source: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  destination: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  processors: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  legal_basis: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  retention_days: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: 730
  },
  encryption_enabled: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: true
  },
  dpia_required: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpia_id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    allowNull: true
  },
  risk_level: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('baixo', 'médio', 'alto'),
    defaultValue: 'médio'
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('ativo', 'inativo', 'revisão'),
    defaultValue: 'ativo'
  },
  last_review_date: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  next_review_date: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: false
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'data_flows',
  timestamps: true,
  hooks: {
    beforeCreate: (flow) => {
      if (!flow.next_review_date) {
        flow.next_review_date = new Date(Date.now() + 365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 1 ano
      }
    }
  }
});

module.exports = DataFlow;
```

## 7. src/models/Consent.js

```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');
const crypto = require('crypto');

const Consent = sequelize.define('Consent', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  consent_id: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    unique: true,
    defaultValue: () => `CONS-${crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex').toUpperCase()}`
  },
  data_subject_id: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    index: true
  },
  data_subject_email: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    validate: {
      isEmail: true
    }
  },
  purpose: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  legal_basis: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  data_categories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: false,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  granted: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  granted_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  granted_ip: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  granted_user_agent: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: true
  },
  withdrawal_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  withdrawal_ip: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  withdrawal_reason: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: true
  },
  version: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    defaultValue: '1.0'
  },
  language: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    defaultValue: 'pt-BR'
  },
  expires_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  metadata: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: {}
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'consents',
  timestamps: true,
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['data_subject_id', 'purpose'],
      unique: true
    }
  ]
});

// Método para verificar consentimento ativo
Consent.prototype.isActive = function() {
  if (!this.granted) return false;
  if (this.withdrawal_at) return false;
  if (this.expires_at && new Date() > this.expires_at) return false;
  return true;
};

// Método para revogar consentimento
Consent.prototype.withdraw = function(ip, userAgent, reason) {
  this.granted = false;
  this.withdrawal_at = new Date();
  this.withdrawal_ip = ip;
  this.withdrawal_user_agent = userAgent;
  this.withdrawal_reason = reason;
  return this.save();
};

module.exports = Consent;
```

## 8. src/models/AuditLog.js

```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');

const AuditLog = sequelize.define('AuditLog', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  event_type: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(
      'consent_granted',
      'consent_withdrawn',
      'data_access',
      'data_modification',
      'data_deletion',
      'data_export',
      'user_login',
      'user_logout',
      'configuration_change',
      'security_incident',
      'compliance_check',
      'dpia_created',
      'incident_notification'
    ),
    allowNull: false
  },
  entity_type: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  entity_id: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  user_id: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  user_role: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  ip_address: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  user_agent: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: true
  },
  description: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  details: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: {}
  },
  severity: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('info', 'warning', 'error', 'critical'),
    defaultValue: 'info'
  },
  compliance_related: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  data_subject_id: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true,
    index: true
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'audit_logs',
  timestamps: true,
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['event_type', 'created_at']
    },
    {
      fields: ['data_subject_id', 'created_at']
    },
    {
      fields: ['compliance_related']
    }
  ]
});

// Método estático para registrar logs
AuditLog.record = async function(event) {
  try {
    return await this.create({
      event_type: event.event_type,
      entity_type: event.entity_type,
      entity_id: event.entity_id,
      user_id: event.user_id,
      user_role: event.user_role,
      ip
