## 1. Terraform Configuration

### `terraform/main.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key    = "production/terraform.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
    encrypt = true
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
    }
  }
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
  }
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "this" {
  name = module.eks.cluster_name
}

module "vpc" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  version = "~> 5.0"

  name = "diyapp-vpc-${var.environment}"
  cidr = var.vpc_cidr

  azs             = var.availability_zones
  private_subnets = var.private_subnets
  public_subnets  = var.public_subnets

  enable_nat_gateway   = true
  single_nat_gateway   = true
  enable_dns_hostnames = true

  tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
  }

  public_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
  }

  private_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
  }
}

module "eks" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  version = "~> 19.0"

  cluster_name    = var.cluster_name
  cluster_version = "1.28"

  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnets

  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    diyapp = {
      min_size     = 3
      max_size     = 10
      desired_size = 3

      instance_types = ["t3.medium"]
      capacity_type  = "SPOT"

      labels = {
        role = "diyapp"
      }

      taints = []

      tags = {
        Environment = var.environment
      }
    }

    monitoring = {
      min_size     = 2
      max_size     = 4
      desired_size = 2

      instance_types = ["t3.large"]
      capacity_type  = "ON_DEMAND"

      labels = {
        role = "monitoring"
      }

      taints = [{
        key    = "role"
        value  = "monitoring"
        effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
      }]

      tags = {
        Environment = var.environment
      }
    }
  }

  node_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_self_all = {
      description = "Node to node all ports/protocols"
      protocol    = "-1"
      from_port   = 0
      to_port     = 0
      type        = "ingress"
      self        = true
    }

    ingress_cluster_ports = {
      description                   = "Cluster API to node group"
      protocol                      = "tcp"
      from_port                     = 1025
      to_port                       = 65535
      type                          = "ingress"
      source_cluster_security_group = true
    }
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
  }
}

module "kubernetes" {
  source = "./modules/kubernetes"

  cluster_name     = module.eks.cluster_name
  cluster_endpoint = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  environment      = var.environment
}

module "monitoring" {
  source = "./modules/monitoring"

  cluster_name     = module.eks.cluster_name
  cluster_endpoint = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  environment      = var.environment
  slack_webhook_url = var.slack_webhook_url
  pagerduty_service_key = var.pagerduty_service_key
}

resource "aws_route53_record" "grafana" {
  zone_id = var.route53_zone_id
  name    = "grafana.${var.domain_name}"
  type    = "CNAME"
  ttl     = 300
  records = [module.eks.cluster_endpoint]
}

resource "aws_route53_record" "prometheus" {
  zone_id = var.route53_zone_id
  name    = "prometheus.${var.domain_name}"
  type    = "CNAME"
  ttl     = 300
  records = [module.eks.cluster_endpoint]
}

resource "aws_route53_record" "alertmanager" {
  zone_id = var.route53_zone_id
  name    = "alertmanager.${var.domain_name}"
  type    = "CNAME"
  ttl     = 300
  records = [module.eks.cluster_endpoint]
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`
```hcl
variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
  default     = "production"
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "EKS cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-v10-cluster"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "Availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
}

variable "private_subnets" {
  description = "Private subnets CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
}

variable "public_subnets" {
  description = "Public subnets CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
}

variable "domain_name" {
  description = "Domain name for the application"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp.example.com"
}

variable "route53_zone_id" {
  description = "Route53 zone ID"
  type        = string
  default     = ""
}

variable "slack_webhook_url" {
  description = "Slack webhook URL for alerts"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
  default     = ""
}

variable "pagerduty_service_key" {
  description = "PagerDuty service key for critical alerts"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
  default     = ""
}

variable "error_budget_threshold" {
  description = "Error budget threshold percentage for alerts"
  type        = number
  default     = 20
}
```

### `terraform/modules/kubernetes/main.tf`
```hcl
resource "kubernetes_namespace" "diyapp" {
  metadata {
    name = "diyapp"
    labels = {
      name = "diyapp"
      environment = var.environment
    }
  }
}

resource "kubernetes_namespace" "monitoring" {
  metadata {
    name = "monitoring"
    labels = {
      name = "monitoring"
      environment = var.environment
    }
  }
}

resource "kubernetes_secret" "diyapp_secrets" {
  metadata {
    name      = "diyapp-secrets"
    namespace = kubernetes_namespace.diyapp.metadata[0].name
  }

  data = {
    DATABASE_URL = var.database_url
    REDIS_URL    = var.redis_url
    JWT_SECRET   = var.jwt_secret
    OPENAI_API_KEY = var.openai_api_key
    ANTHROPIC_API_KEY = var.anthropic_api_key
    GOOGLE_API_KEY = var.google_api_key
  }

  type = "Opaque"
}

resource "kubernetes_config_map" "diyapp_config" {
  metadata {
    name      = "diyapp-config"
    namespace = kubernetes_namespace.diyapp.metadata[0].name
  }

  data = {
    NODE_ENV           = var.environment
    LOG_LEVEL          = "info"
    API_PORT           = "3000"
    CORS_ORIGIN        = "*"
    RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW  = "900000"
    RATE_LIMIT_MAX     = "100"
    LLM_TIMEOUT        = "30000"
    LLM_MAX_TOKENS     = "4096"
  }
}
```

### `kubernetes/diyapp/deployment.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v10
    component: api
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v10
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "3000"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: diyapp-api
        image: diyapp/api:v10
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-config
              key: NODE_ENV
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-config
              key: LOG_LEVEL
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: DATABASE_URL
        - name: OPENAI_API_KEY
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: OPENAI_API_KEY
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "1Gi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 1
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 30
        volumeMounts:
        - name: logs
          mountPath: /var/log/diyapp
      volumes:
      - name: logs
        emptyDir: {}
      nodeSelector:
        role: diyapp
      tolerations:
      - key: "role"
        operator: "Equal"
        value: "diyapp"
        effect: "NoSchedule"
---
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-worker
  namespace: diyapp
  labels:
    app: diyapp-worker
    version: v10
    component: worker
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-worker
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-worker
        version: v10
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: diyapp-worker
        image: diyapp/worker:v10
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-config
              key: NODE_ENV
        - name: REDIS_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: REDIS_URL
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "100m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
        volumeMounts:
        - name: logs
          mountPath: /var/log/diyapp
      volumes:
      - name: logs
        emptyDir: {}
      nodeSelector:
        role: diyapp
      tolerations:
      - key: "role"
        operator: "Equal"
        value: "diyapp"
        effect: "NoSchedule"
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Data Engineering Optimization

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-data/
├── README.md
├── docker-compose.yml
├── dbt/
│   ├── models/

│   │   └── sources.yml

│   ├── dags/

## 1. docker-compose.yml - Infraestrutura de Dados

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Data Warehouse (PostgreSQL para simulação - produção seria BigQuery/Snowflake)
  postgres-dw:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_dw
      POSTGRES_USER: data_engineer
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DW_PASSWORD:-secure_password_123}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init_warehouse.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U data_engineer"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Airflow - Orquestração
  airflow-webserver:
    build: ./airflow
    command: webserver
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__DATABASE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres-airflow/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
    depends_on:
      postgres-airflow:
        condition: service_healthy

  airflow-scheduler:
    build: ./airflow
    command: scheduler
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__DATABASE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres-airflow/airflow
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
    depends_on:
      - airflow-webserver

  postgres-airflow:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: airflow
      POSTGRES_USER: airflow
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: airflow
    volumes:
      - postgres_airflow_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  # Metabase - Visualização
  metabase:
    image: metabase/metabase:latest
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      MB_DB_TYPE: postgres
      MB_DB_DBNAME: metabase
      MB_DB_PORT: 5432
      MB_DB_USER: metabase
      MB_DB_PASS: ${METABASE_PASSWORD:-secure_password_456}
      MB_DB_HOST: postgres-metabase
    depends_on:
      postgres-metabase:
        condition: service_healthy

  postgres-metabase:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: metabase
      POSTGRES_USER: metabase
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${METABASE_PASSWORD:-secure_password_456}
    volumes:
      - metabase_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  postgres_airflow_data:
  metabase_data:
```

## 2. dbt/dbt_project.yml - Configuração do Projeto dbt

```yaml
name: 'diyapp_v10'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_v10'

model-paths: ["models"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
seed-paths: ["data"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v10:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      schema: staging
      tags: ['staging']
    marts:
      materialized: table
      schema: marts
      tags: ['marts']
      product:
        materialized: table
        schema: product_marts
        tags: ['product', 'marts']
      ai:
        materialized: table
        schema: ai_marts
        tags: ['ai', 'marts']
      ops:
        materialized: table
        schema: ops_marts
        tags: ['ops', 'marts']

seeds:
  diyapp_v10:
    quote_columns: false

tests:
  diyapp_v10:
    data_quality:
      warn_if: "> 0"
      error_if: "> 5"
```

## 3. dbt/models/sources.yml - Definição das Fontes de Dados

```yaml
version: 2

sources:
  - name: diyapp_production
    database: diyapp_prod_db
    schema: public
    tables:
      - name: user_events
        description: "Eventos de usuário do produto DIYAPP"
        loaded_at_field: created_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
        columns:
          - name: event_id
            tests:
              - unique
              - not_null
          - name: user_id
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: event_type
            tests:
              - not_null
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['login', 'feature_used', 'payment', 'error', 'session_start']
          - name: event_data
            description: "JSON com dados específicos do evento"
          - name: created_at
            tests:
              - not_null

      - name: llm_calls
        description: "Logs de chamadas ao LLM Gateway"
        loaded_at_field: timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 5, period: minute}
          error_after: {count: 15, period: minute}
        columns:
          - name: call_id
            tests:
              - unique
              - not_null
          - name: feature_name
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: model_used
          - name: provider
          - name: tokens_input
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: tokens_output
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: cost_usd
          - name: latency_ms
          - name: timestamp
            tests:
              - not_null

      - name: deployments
        description: "Registros de deploy da aplicação"
        loaded_at_field: deployed_at
        columns:
          - name: deployment_id
            tests:
              - unique
              - not_null
          - name: version
          - name: status
            tests:
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['success', 'failed', 'rolled_back']
          - name: deployed_at
            tests:
              - not_null

      - name: incidents
        description: "Incidentes e alertas do sistema"
        loaded_at_field: created_at
        columns:
          - name: incident_id
            tests:
              - unique
              - not_null
          - name: severity
            tests:
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['critical', 'high', 'medium', 'low']
          - name: service
          - name: resolved_at
          - name: created_at
            tests:
              - not_null
```

## 4. dbt/models/staging/stg_user_events.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'events']
    )
}}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        -- Parse JSON fields
        (event_data->>'feature_name')::VARCHAR AS feature_name,
        (event_data->>'duration_ms')::INTEGER AS duration_ms,
        (event_data->>'success')::BOOLEAN AS success,
        (event_data->>'error_code')::VARCHAR AS error_code,
        created_at,
        DATE(created_at) AS event_date,
        -- Add ingestion metadata
        CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS _loaded_at,
        '{{ invocation_id }}' AS _batch_id
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_production', 'user_events') }}
    WHERE created_at >= DATEADD('day', -30, CURRENT_DATE) -- Last 30 days for performance
),

enriched AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        -- Business logic: session_id from consecutive events within 30 minutes
        CASE
            WHEN LAG(created_at) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY created_at) 
                 IS NULL OR 
                 DATEDIFF('minute', LAG(created_at) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY created_at), created_at) > 30
            THEN MD5(CONCAT(user_id, created_at::DATE, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY created_at)))
            ELSE LAG(MD5(CONCAT(user_id, created_at::DATE, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY created_at)))) 
                 OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY created_at)
        END AS session_id
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM enriched
```

## 5. dbt/models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'llm', 'cost']
    )
}}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        feature_name,
        model_used,
        provider,
        tokens_input,
        tokens_output,
        tokens_input + tokens_output AS total_tokens,
        cost_usd,
        -- Calculate cost per token for monitoring
        CASE 
            WHEN (tokens_input + tokens_output) > 0 
            THEN cost_usd / (tokens_input + tokens_output)
            ELSE 0 
        END AS cost_per_token_usd,
        latency_ms,
        timestamp,
        DATE(timestamp) AS call_date,
        HOUR(timestamp) AS call_hour,
        -- SLA compliance check
        CASE 
            WHEN latency_ms <= 1000 THEN 'within_sla'
            WHEN latency_ms <= 2000 THEN 'warning'
            ELSE 'violation'
        END AS sla_status,
        CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS _loaded_at,
        '{{ invocation_id }}' AS _batch_id
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_production', 'llm_calls') }}
    WHERE timestamp >= DATEADD('hour', -24, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP) -- Last 24 hours for near real-time
),

quality_checks AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        -- Data quality flags
        CASE 
            WHEN tokens_input < 0 THEN TRUE 
            ELSE FALSE 
        END AS is_negative_tokens,
        CASE 
            WHEN cost_usd < 0 THEN TRUE 
            ELSE FALSE 
        END AS is_negative_cost,
        CASE 
            WHEN latency_ms < 0 THEN TRUE 
            ELSE FALSE 
        END AS is_negative_latency
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM quality_checks
```

## 6. dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='product_marts',
        tags=['product', 'marts', 'kpi'],
        partition_by={
            "field": "event_date",
            "data_type": "date",
            "granularity": "day"
        },
        cluster_by=["user_segment"]
    )
}}

WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        event_date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS daily_sessions,
        COUNT(*) AS total_events,
        COUNT(DISTINCT feature_name) AS features_used,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_type = 'feature_used' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS feature_usage_count,
        AVG(duration_ms) AS avg_session_duration_ms,
        MAX(created_at) AS last_event_time
    FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
    WHERE event_date = DATEADD('day', -1, CURRENT_DATE) -- Yesterday's data
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

user_segmentation AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        event_date,
        daily_sessions,
        total_events,
        features_used,
        feature_usage_count,
        avg_session_duration_ms,
        last_event_time,
        -- User segmentation
        CASE
            WHEN daily_sessions >= 3 AND features_used >= 2 THEN 'power_user'
            WHEN daily_sessions >= 1 THEN 'active_user'
            ELSE 'light_user'
        END AS user_segment,
        -- Retention cohort (days since first seen)
        DATEDIFF('day', MIN(event_date) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id), event_date) AS days_since_first_seen
    FROM daily_events
),

cohort_analysis AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        -- Weekly cohort
        DATE_TRUNC('week', MIN(event_date) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id)) AS acquisition_week,
        -- Monthly cohort
        DATE_TRUNC('month', MIN(event_date) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id)) AS acquisition_month
    FROM user_segmentation
)

SELECT
    event_date,
    user_id,
    user_segment,
    daily_sessions,
    total_events,
    features_used,
    feature_usage_count,
    avg_session_duration_ms,
    days_since_first_seen,
    acquisition_week,
    acquisition_month,
    last_event_time,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS _calculated_at
FROM cohort_analysis
```

## 7. dbt/models/marts/ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='ai_marts',
        tags=['ai', 'marts', 'cost', 'llm'],
        partition_by={
            "field": "call_date",
            "data_type": "date",
            "granularity": "day"
        },
        cluster_by=["feature_name", "provider"]
    )
}}

WITH hourly_aggregates AS (
    SELECT
        call_date,
        call_hour,
        feature_name,
        model_used,
        provider,
        COUNT(*) AS total_calls,
        SUM(tokens_input) AS total_tokens_input,
        SUM(tokens_output) AS total_tokens_output,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens_all,
        SUM(cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(cost_per_token_usd) AS avg_cost_per_token_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) AS p95_latency_ms,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sla_status = 'violation' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS sla_violations,
        SUM(CASE WHEN is_negative_tokens THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS data_quality_issues
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE call_date >= DATEADD('day', -7, CURRENT_DATE) -- Last 7 days
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4, 5
),

feature_trends AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        -- 7-day moving average for anomaly detection
        AVG(total_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, provider 
            ORDER BY call_date, call_hour 
            ROWS BETWEEN 168 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW -- 7 days * 24 hours
        ) AS avg_cost_7d,
        -- Cost per call trend
        total_cost_usd / NULLIF(total_calls, 0) AS cost_per_call,
        -- Token efficiency
        total_tokens_output / NULLIF(total_tokens_input, 0) AS token_efficiency_ratio
    FROM hourly_aggregates
),

budget_monitoring AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        -- Budget alerts (assuming $1000 daily budget per feature)
        CASE
            WHEN total_cost_usd > 1000 THEN 'over_budget'
            WHEN total_cost_usd > 800 THEN 'near_budget'
            ELSE 'within_budget'
        END AS budget_status,
        -- Provider cost comparison
        AVG(total_cost_usd) OVER (PARTITION BY feature_name, call_date) AS avg_feature_cost_daily,
        total_cost_usd / NULLIF(AVG(total_cost_usd) OVER (PARTITION BY feature_name, call_date), 0) AS cost_ratio_to_avg
    FROM feature_trends
)

SELECT
    call_date,
    call_hour,
    feature_name,
    model_used,
    provider,
    total_calls,
    total_tokens_input,
    total_tokens_output,
    total_tokens_all,
    total_cost_usd,
    avg_cost_per_token_usd,
    avg_latency_ms,
    p95_latency_ms,
    sla_violations,
    data_quality_issues,
    avg_cost_7d,
    cost_per_call,
    token_efficiency_ratio,
    budget_status,
    avg_feature_cost_daily,
    cost_ratio_to_avg,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS _calculated_at
FROM budget_monitoring
```

```javascript

const securityAuditReport = {

## 2. Implementação de Autenticação OAuth2.0/JWT

### 2.1. Configuração de Segurança

```javascript
// config/security.js
require('dotenv').config();

module.exports = {
  // JWT Configuration
  jwt: {
    accessTokenSecret: process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET || 'fallback-secret-change-in-production',
    refreshTokenSecret: process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || 'fallback-refresh-secret-change',
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m', // 15 minutos
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d', // 7 dias
    issuer: 'diyapp-v10',
    audience: 'diyapp-users'
  },
  
  // OAuth2 Providers
  oauth: {
    google: {
      clientId: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET,
      redirectUri: process.env.GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI || 'http://localhost:3000/auth/google/callback'
    },
    github: {
      clientId: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_ID,
      clientSecret: process.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET,
      redirectUri: process.env.GITHUB_REDIRECT_URI || 'http://localhost:3000/auth/github/callback'
    }
  },
  
  // Password Policy
  passwordPolicy: {
    minLength: 12,
    requireUppercase: true,
    requireLowercase: true,
    requireNumbers: true,
    requireSpecialChars: true,
    maxAgeDays: 90, // Rotação obrigatória a cada 90 dias
    historySize: 5 // Não pode reutilizar as últimas 5 senhas
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimits: {
    auth: {
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 5, // 5 tentativas por IP
      message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later'
    },
    api: {
      windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minuto
      max: 100 // 100 requisições por minuto
    }
  }
};
```

### 2.2. Serviço de Autenticação JWT

```javascript
// services/auth/jwt-service.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../../config/security');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');

class JWTService {
  constructor() {
    this.blacklist = new Set();
  }
  
  /**
   * Gera access token JWT
   */
  generateAccessToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      roles: user.roles || ['user'],
      permissions: user.permissions || [],
      iss: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
      aud: securityConfig.jwt.audience,
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
    };
    
    return jwt.sign(payload, securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenExpiry
    });
  }
  
  /**
   * Gera refresh token com maior expiração
   */
  generateRefreshToken(userId) {
    const payload = {
      sub: userId,
      tokenId: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      type: 'refresh'
    };
    
    return jwt.sign(payload, securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenExpiry
    });
  }
  
  /**
   * Verifica access token
   */
  verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenSecret, {
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(`Token verification failed: ${error.message}`);
      return null;
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * Verifica refresh token
   */
  verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenSecret);
      
      // Verifica se token está na blacklist
      if (this.blacklist.has(decoded.tokenId)) {
        throw new Error('Token revoked');
      }
      
      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(`Refresh token verification failed: ${error.message}`);
      return null;
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * Revoga refresh token
   */
  revokeRefreshToken(tokenId) {
    this.blacklist.add(tokenId);
    
    // Limpa blacklist antiga periodicamente (em produção usar Redis)
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.blacklist.delete(tokenId);
    }, 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 7 dias
  }
  
  /**
   * Rotação de tokens
   */
  rotateTokens(oldRefreshToken) {
    const decoded = this.verifyRefreshToken(oldRefreshToken);
    if (!decoded) {
      throw new Error('Invalid refresh token');
    }
    
    // Revoga token antigo
    this.revokeRefreshToken(decoded.tokenId);
    
    // Gera novos tokens
    const newAccessToken = this.generateAccessToken({ id: decoded.sub });
    const newRefreshToken = this.generateRefreshToken(decoded.sub);
    
    return {
      accessToken: newAccessToken,
      refreshToken: newRefreshToken
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTService();
```

### 2.3. Middleware de Autenticação

```javascript
// middleware/auth-middleware.js
const jwtService = require('../services/auth/jwt-service');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class AuthMiddleware {
  /**
   * Middleware para verificar JWT
   */
  authenticate(req, res, next) {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Authentication required',
        code: 'AUTH_REQUIRED'
      });
    }
    
    const token = authHeader.substring(7);
    const decoded = jwtService.verifyAccessToken(token);
    
    if (!decoded) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Invalid or expired token',
        code: 'INVALID_TOKEN'
      });
    }
    
    // Adiciona usuário ao request
    req.user = {
      id: decoded.sub,
      email: decoded.email,
      roles: decoded.roles,
      permissions: decoded.permissions
    };
    
    // Log de acesso
    logger.info(`User ${req.user.id} accessed ${req.method} ${req.path}`);
    
    next();
  }
  
  /**
   * Middleware para verificar roles
   */
  requireRole(requiredRoles) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!req.user) {
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
      }
      
      const hasRole = requiredRoles.some(role => 
        req.user.roles.includes(role)
      );
      
      if (!hasRole) {
        logger.warn(`User ${req.user.id} attempted unauthorized access to ${req.path}`);
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Insufficient permissions',
          code: 'FORBIDDEN'
        });
      }
      
      next();
    };
  }
  
  /**
   * Middleware para verificar permissões específicas
   */
  requirePermission(requiredPermissions) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!req.user) {
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
      }
      
      const hasPermission = requiredPermissions.every(permission =>
        req.user.permissions.includes(permission)
      );
      
      if (!hasPermission) {
        logger.warn(`User ${req.user.id} missing permissions for ${req.path}`);
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Insufficient permissions',
          code: 'FORBIDDEN'
        });
      }
      
      next();
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new AuthMiddleware();
```

### 2.4. Controlador de Autenticação OAuth2

```javascript
// controllers/auth-controller.js
const axios = require('axios');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const jwtService = require('../services/auth/jwt-service');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const UserService = require('../services/user-service');

class AuthController {
  /**
   * Gera estado OAuth2 para prevenção de CSRF
   */
  generateOAuthState() {
    return crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
  }
  
  /**
   * Inicia fluxo OAuth2 do Google
   */
  async startGoogleOAuth(req, res) {
    const state = this.generateOAuthState();
    
    // Armazena estado na sessão
    req.session.oauthState = state;
    
    const authUrl = new URL('https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth');
    authUrl.searchParams.append('client_id', securityConfig.oauth.google.clientId);
    authUrl.searchParams.append('redirect_uri', securityConfig.oauth.google.redirectUri);
    authUrl.searchParams.append('response_type', 'code');
    authUrl.searchParams.append('scope', 'email profile');
    authUrl.searchParams.append('state', state);
    authUrl.searchParams.append('access_type', 'offline');
    authUrl.searchParams.append('prompt', 'consent');
    
    res.redirect(authUrl.toString());
  }
  
  /**
   * Callback do Google OAuth2
   */
  async handleGoogleCallback(req, res) {
    const { code, state } = req.query;
    
    // Verifica estado para prevenção de CSRF
    if (!state || state !== req.session.oauthState) {
      logger.warn('OAuth state mismatch - possible CSRF attack');
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid state parameter' });
    }
    
    try {
      // Troca código por access token
      const tokenResponse = await axios.post('https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token', {
        code,
        client_id: securityConfig.oauth.google.clientId,
        client_secret: securityConfig.oauth.google.clientSecret,
        redirect_uri: securityConfig.oauth.google.redirectUri,
        grant_type: 'authorization_code'
      });
      
      // Obtém informações do usuário
      const userInfoResponse = await axios.get('https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v2/userinfo', {
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${tokenResponse.data.access_token}`
        }
      });
      
      const userInfo = userInfoResponse.data;
      
      // Cria ou atualiza usuário
      const user = await UserService.findOrCreateFromOAuth({
        provider: 'google',
        providerId: userInfo.id,
        email: userInfo.email,
        name: userInfo.name,
        picture: userInfo.picture
      });
      
      // Gera tokens JWT
      const accessToken = jwtService.generateAccessToken(user);
      const refreshToken = jwtService.generateRefreshToken(user.id);
      
      // Limpa estado da sessão
      delete req.session.oauthState;
      
      // Retorna tokens
      res.json({
        accessToken,
        refreshToken,
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name
        }
      });
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Google OAuth callback failed: ${error.message}`);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Authentication failed' });
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * Login com email/senha
   */
  async login(req, res) {
    const { email, password } = req.body;
    
    try {
      // Validação de input
      if (!email || !password) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email and password required' });
      }
      
      // Busca usuário
      const user = await UserService.findByEmail(email);
      if (!user) {
        logger.warn(`Failed login attempt for non-existent email: ${email}`);
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
      }
      
      // Verifica senha
      const isValid = await UserService.verifyPassword(password, user.passwordHash);
      if (!isValid) {
        logger.warn(`Failed login attempt for user: ${user.id}`);
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
      }
      
      // Verifica se conta está bloqueada
      if (user.isLocked) {
        return res.status(423).json({ error: 'Account is locked' });
      }
      
      // Gera tokens
      const accessToken = jwtService.generateAccessToken(user);
      const refreshToken = jwtService.generateRefreshToken(user.id);
      
      // Log de login bem-sucedido
      logger.info(`User ${user.id} logged in successfully`);
      
      res.json({
        accessToken,
        refreshToken,
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name,
          roles: user.roles
        }
      });
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Login failed: ${error.message}`);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Login failed' });
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * Refresh token
   */
  async refreshToken(req, res) {
    const { refreshToken } = req.body;
    
    if (!refreshToken) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Refresh token required' });
    }
    
    try {
      const tokens = jwtService.rotateTokens(refreshToken);
      res.json(tokens);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(`Token refresh failed: ${error.message}`);
      res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid refresh token' });
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * Logout
   */
  async logout(req, res) {
    const { refreshToken } = req.body;
    
    if (refreshToken) {
      try {
        const decoded = jwt.decode(refreshToken);
        if (decoded && decoded.tokenId) {
          jwtService.revokeRefreshToken(decoded.tokenId);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        // Continua mesmo se token for inválido
      }
    }
    
    logger.info(`User ${req.user?.id} logged out`);
    res.json({ message: 'Logged out successfully' });
  }
}

module.exports = new AuthController();
```

// utils/input-sanitizer.js
const DOMPurify = require('isomorphic-dompurify');
const validator = require('validator');
const logger = require('./logger');

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    // Configuração DOMPurify
    DOMPurify.setConfig({
      ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'a', 'p', 'br', 'ul', 'ol', 'li'],
      ALLOWED_ATTR: ['href', 'target'],
      ALLOW_DATA_ATTR: false
    });
  }
  
  /**
   * Sanitiza string HTML
   */
  sanitizeHTML(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    return DOMPurify.sanitize(input);
  }
  
  /**
   * Val

  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1"
  }
}
```

## 2. Banco de Dados - Migrações

### src/database/migrations/001_create_compliance_tables.sql
```sql
-- Tabela de Atividades de Processamento (ROPA - LGPD Art. 37)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS data_processing_activities (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    activity_name TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
    data_categories TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(legal_basis IN ('consent', 'contract', 'legal_obligation', 'vital_interest', 'public_interest', 'legitimate_interest')),
    data_subjects TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    retention_period_days INTEGER NOT NULL,
    data_controllers TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    data_processors TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    international_transfers BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    transfer_mechanism TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE
);

-- Tabela de Consentimentos
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS consents (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    consent_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
    data_categories TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    granted_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    expires_at TIMESTAMP,
    version TEXT NOT NULL,
    consent_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    ip_address TEXT,
    user_agent TEXT,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    revoked_at TIMESTAMP,
    revocation_reason TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(user_id, consent_type, version)
);

-- Tabela de Solicitações de Titulares
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS data_subject_requests (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    request_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(request_type IN ('access', 'rectification', 'erasure', 'restriction', 'portability', 'objection')),
    status TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(status IN ('received', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'rejected', 'cancelled')) DEFAULT 'received',
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    requested_data TEXT, -- JSON array
    response_data TEXT, -- JSON para dados retornados
    received_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deadline_at TIMESTAMP GENERATED ALWAYS AS (datetime(received_at, '+15 days')),
    completed_at TIMESTAMP,
    rejection_reason TEXT,
    dpo_notes TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela de Logs de Auditoria
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_logs (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    event_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    event_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(event_type IN ('consent_granted', 'consent_revoked', 'data_access', 'data_modification', 'data_deletion', 'data_export', 'incident', 'configuration_change', 'user_action')),
    user_id TEXT,
    user_role TEXT,
    ip_address TEXT,
    user_agent TEXT,
    resource_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    resource_id TEXT,
    action TEXT NOT NULL,
    details TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON
    timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    compliance_related BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    retention_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE
);

-- Tabela de DPIAs
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dpias (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    feature_name TEXT NOT NULL,
    feature_description TEXT NOT NULL,
    data_categories TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    processing_purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
    legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL,
    data_subjects_count INTEGER,
    risk_assessment TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON
    mitigation_measures TEXT NOT NULL, -- JSON array
    llm_usage BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    llm_provider TEXT,
    llm_dpa_signed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    eu_ai_act_classification TEXT,
    approval_status TEXT CHECK(approval_status IN ('pending', 'approved', 'rejected', 'approved_with_conditions')) DEFAULT 'pending',
    approved_by TEXT,
    approved_at TIMESTAMP,
    review_date TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela de Incidentes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS security_incidents (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    incident_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    incident_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(incident_type IN ('data_breach', 'unauthorized_access', 'data_loss', 'system_compromise', 'other')),
    severity TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(severity IN ('low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical')),
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    affected_data_categories TEXT, -- JSON array
    affected_subjects_count INTEGER,
    detected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    contained_at TIMESTAMP,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
    notification_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    notified_authority_at TIMESTAMP,
    notified_subjects_at TIMESTAMP,
    notification_details TEXT, -- JSON
    root_cause TEXT,
    corrective_actions TEXT, -- JSON array
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Índices para performance
CREATE INDEX idx_consents_user_id ON consents(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_consents_active ON consents(is_active);
CREATE INDEX idx_requests_user_id ON data_subject_requests(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_requests_status ON data_subject_requests(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_requests_deadline ON data_subject_requests(deadline_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_user_id ON audit_logs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_timestamp ON audit_logs(timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_compliance ON audit_logs(compliance_related);
CREATE INDEX idx_dpias_status ON dpias(approval_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_incidents_detected ON security_incidents(detected_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_incidents_severity ON security_incidents(severity);

-- Trigger para atualizar updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS update_data_processing_activities_timestamp 
AFTER UPDATE ON data_processing_activities 
BEGIN
    UPDATE data_processing_activities SET updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP WHERE id = NEW.id;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS update_consents_timestamp 
AFTER UPDATE ON consents 
BEGIN
    UPDATE consents SET updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP WHERE id = NEW.id;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS update_data_subject_requests_timestamp 
AFTER UPDATE ON data_subject_requests 
BEGIN
    UPDATE data_subject_requests SET updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP WHERE id = NEW.id;
END;
```

### src/database/connection.js
```javascript
const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose();
const path = require('path');
require('dotenv').config();

class Database {
    constructor() {
        this.dbPath = process.env.DB_PATH || './database/compliance.db';
        this.db = null;
    }

    connect() {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.db = new sqlite3.Database(
                this.dbPath,
                sqlite3.OPEN_READWRITE | sqlite3.OPEN_CREATE,
                (err) => {
                    if (err) {
                        console.error('Erro ao conectar ao banco de dados:', err);
                        reject(err);
                    } else {
                        console.log('Conectado ao banco de dados de compliance');
                        this.enableForeignKeys();
                        resolve(this.db);
                    }
                }
            );
        });
    }

    enableForeignKeys() {
        this.db.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON');
    }

    run(sql, params = []) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.db.run(sql, params, function(err) {
                if (err) {
                    reject(err);
                } else {
                    resolve({ id: this.lastID, changes: this.changes });
                }
            });
        });
    }

    get(sql, params = []) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.db.get(sql, params, (err, row) => {
                if (err) {
                    reject(err);
                } else {
                    resolve(row);
                }
            });
        });
    }

    all(sql, params = []) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.db.all(sql, params, (err, rows) => {
                if (err) {
                    reject(err);
                } else {
                    resolve(rows);
                }
            });
        });
    }

    close() {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.db.close((err) => {
                if (err) {
                    reject(err);
                } else {
                    resolve();
                }
            });
        });
    }
}

module.exports = new Database();
```

## 3. Modelos de Dados

### src/compliance/models/DataProcessingActivity.js
```javascript
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../database/connection');

class DataProcessingActivity {
    constructor(data) {
        this.id = data.id || uuidv4();
        this.activity_name = data.activity_name;
        this.description = data.description;
        this.purpose = data.purpose;
        this.data_categories = Array.isArray(data.data_categories) 
            ? JSON.stringify(data.data_categories) 
            : data.data_categories;
        this.legal_basis = data.legal_basis;
        this.data_subjects = Array.isArray(data.data_subjects)
            ? JSON.stringify(data.data_subjects)
            : data.data_subjects;
        this.retention_period_days = data.retention_period_days;
        this.data_controllers = Array.isArray(data.data_controllers)
            ? JSON.stringify(data.data_controllers)
            : data.data_controllers;
        this.data_processors = Array.isArray(data.data_processors)
            ? JSON.stringify(data.data_processors)
            : data.data_processors;
        this.international_transfers = data.international_transfers || false;
        this.transfer_mechanism = data.transfer_mechanism;
        this.is_active = data.is_active !== undefined ? data.is_active : true;
    }

    static async create(activityData) {
        const activity = new DataProcessingActivity(activityData);
        
        const sql = `
            INSERT INTO data_processing_activities 
            (id, activity_name, description, purpose, data_categories, legal_basis, 
             data_subjects, retention_period_days, data_controllers, data_processors,
             international_transfers, transfer_mechanism, is_active)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        `;
        
        const params = [
            activity.id, activity.activity_name, activity.description, 
            activity.purpose, activity.data_categories, activity.legal_basis,
            activity.data_subjects, activity.retention_period_days,
            activity.data_controllers, activity.data_processors,
            activity.international_transfers, activity.transfer_mechanism,
            activity.is_active
        ];
        
        await db.run(sql, params);
        return activity;
    }

    static async findById(id) {
        const sql = 'SELECT * FROM data_processing_activities WHERE id = ?';
        const row = await db.get(sql, [id]);
        
        if (row) {
            row.data_categories = JSON.parse(row.data_categories);
            row.data_subjects = JSON.parse(row.data_subjects);
            row.data_controllers = JSON.parse(row.data_controllers);
            row.data_processors = JSON.parse(row.data_processors);
        }
        
        return row;
    }

    static async findAll(activeOnly = true) {
        const sql = activeOnly 
            ? 'SELECT * FROM data_processing_activities WHERE is_active = TRUE ORDER BY created_at DESC'
            : 'SELECT * FROM data_processing_activities ORDER BY created_at DESC';
        
        const rows = await db.all(sql);
        
        return rows.map(row => {
            row.data_categories = JSON.parse(row.data_categories);
            row.data_subjects = JSON.parse(row.data_subjects);
            row.data_controllers = JSON.parse(row.data_controllers);
            row.data_processors = JSON.parse(row.data_processors);
            return row;
        });
    }

    static async update(id, updates) {
        const allowedFields = [
            'activity_name', 'description', 'purpose', 'data_categories',
            'legal_basis', 'data_subjects', 'retention_period_days',
            'data_controllers', 'data_processors', 'international_transfers',
            'transfer_mechanism', 'is_active'
        ];
        
        const setClause = [];
        const params = [];
        
        allowedFields.forEach(field => {
            if (updates[field] !== undefined) {
                setClause.push(`${field} = ?`);
                params.push(
                    Array.isArray(updates[field]) 
                        ? JSON.stringify(updates[field]) 
                        : updates[field]
                );
            }
        });
        
        if (setClause.length === 0) {
            throw new Error('Nenhum campo válido para atualização');
        }
        
        params.push(id);
        
        const sql = `
            UPDATE data_processing_activities 
            SET ${setClause.join(', ')} 
            WHERE id = ?
        `;
        
        await db.run(sql, params);
        return this.findById(id);
    }

    static async delete(id) {
        const sql = 'UPDATE data_processing_activities SET is_active = FALSE WHERE id = ?';
        await db.run(sql, [id]);
        return true;
    }

    static async getROPAReport() {
        const sql = `
            SELECT 
                activity_name,
                purpose,
                legal_basis,
                json_array_length(data_categories) as data_categories_count,
                json_array_length(data_subjects) as data_subjects_count,
                retention_period_days,
                international_transfers,
                created_at,
                updated_at
            FROM data_processing_activities 
            WHERE is_active = TRUE
            ORDER BY activity_name
        `;
        
        return await db.all(sql);
    }
}

module.exports = DataProcessingActivity;
```

            ? JSON.stringify(data.data_categories

```javascript
const { defineConfig } = require('cypress')

module.exports = defineConfig({
  projectId: 'diyapp-v10',
  viewportWidth: 1920,
  viewportHeight: 1080,
  defaultCommandTimeout: 10000,
  requestTimeout: 15000,
  responseTimeout: 15000,
  video: true,
  videoCompression: 32,
  screenshotOnRunFailure: true,
  trashAssetsBeforeRuns: true,
  
  env: {
    apiUrl: 'http://localhost:3000/api',
    llmApiUrl: 'http://localhost:3001/api',
    adminEmail: 'admin@diyapp.com',
    adminPassword: process.env.TEST_ADMIN_PASSWORD,
    testUserEmail: 'test.user@diyapp.com',
    testUserPassword: process.env.TEST_USER_PASSWORD,
  },
  
  e2e: {
    baseUrl: 'http://localhost:3000',
    specPattern: 'tests/e2e/cypress/e2e/**/*.cy.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}',
    supportFile: 'tests/e2e/cypress/support/e2e.js',
    fixturesFolder: 'tests/e2e/cypress/fixtures',
    experimentalRunAllSpecs: true,
    experimentalMemoryManagement: true,
    
    setupNodeEvents(on, config) {
      on('task', {
        log(message) {
          console.log(message)
          return null
        },
        
        table(message) {
          console.table(message)
          return null
        },
        
        generateTestData() {
          return {
            timestamp: Date.now(),
            randomString: Math.random().toString(36).substring(7),
            testId: `test_${Date.now()}_${Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000)}`
          }
        }
      })
      
      // Load environment-specific config
      const environment = config.env.environment || 'local'
      const envConfig = require(`../../config/environments.json`)[environment]
      
      return {
        ...config,
        ...envConfig
      }
    }
  },
  
  retries: {
    runMode: 2,
    openMode: 0
  }
})
